# Kernen i strategy-laget

En strategi skal ikke bare være et navn som:

```text
Defensive
Balanced
Aggressive
```

Den skal være en **konfiguration**, som påvirker:

```text
1. Hvilke actions er tilladt?
2. Hvordan scores IQN-output?
3. Hvor meget vægtes downside risk?
4. Hvor meget cash bør porteføljen have?
5. Hvor stor må én position være?
6. Hvornår er rebalance nødvendigt?
7. Hvordan evalueres resultatet?
8. Hvad logges i audit trail?
```

Så strategy-laget er broen mellem:

```text
Investor preference
↓
DSS decision logic
↓
IQN action selection
↓
Portfolio constraints
```

---

# Minimal V2: 3 hardcoded strategier

Jeg ville lave disse tre:

```text
1. Defensive Preservation
2. Balanced Growth
3. Aggressive Growth
```

De skal alle være long-only, ingen shorting, ingen margin.

---

## 1. Defensive Preservation

Formål:

```text
Bevar kapital, reducer drawdown, undgå høj koncentration.
```

Passer til investor, der hellere vil misse noget upside end tage stor downside.

```python
DEFENSIVE_PRESERVATION = {
    "strategy_id": "defensive_preservation",
    "display_name": "Defensive Preservation",
    "risk_profile": "low",
    "objective": "capital_preservation",

    "constraints": {
        "allow_shorting": False,
        "allow_margin": False,
        "max_position_weight": 0.15,
        "max_sector_weight": 0.35,
        "min_cash_weight": 0.15,
        "target_cash_weight": 0.20,
        "max_turnover_per_decision": 0.20,
    },

    "risk_policy": {
        "lambda_cvar": 1.50,
        "lambda_drawdown": 1.25,
        "lambda_volatility": 1.00,
        "lambda_transaction_cost": 0.50,
        "lambda_concentration": 1.25,
        "lambda_strategy_violation": 2.00,
        "score_quantile": "q50",
        "downside_metric": "cvar10",
    },

    "allowed_actions": [
        "HOLD",
        "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25",
        "INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET",
        "ADD_TO_LOWEST_RISK_5",
    ],

    "rebalance": {
        "frequency": "monthly",
        "drift_threshold": 0.05,
        "force_if_position_above_max": True,
    },

    "evaluation_metrics": [
        "total_return",
        "max_drawdown",
        "cvar10",
        "volatility",
        "sharpe",
    ],
}
```

---

## 2. Balanced Growth

Formål:

```text
Balancér vækst og risiko. Tillad moderat upside, men kontroller drawdown og koncentration.
```

Det her bør nok være din default-strategi.

```python
BALANCED_GROWTH = {
    "strategy_id": "balanced_growth",
    "display_name": "Balanced Growth",
    "risk_profile": "medium",
    "objective": "risk_adjusted_growth",

    "constraints": {
        "allow_shorting": False,
        "allow_margin": False,
        "max_position_weight": 0.25,
        "max_sector_weight": 0.50,
        "min_cash_weight": 0.05,
        "target_cash_weight": 0.10,
        "max_turnover_per_decision": 0.35,
    },

    "risk_policy": {
        "lambda_cvar": 0.75,
        "lambda_drawdown": 0.75,
        "lambda_volatility": 0.50,
        "lambda_transaction_cost": 0.35,
        "lambda_concentration": 0.75,
        "lambda_strategy_violation": 1.50,
        "score_quantile": "q50",
        "downside_metric": "cvar10",
    },

    "allowed_actions": [
        "HOLD",
        "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25",
        "INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET",
        "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5",
        "ADD_TO_LOWEST_RISK_5",
        "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_5",
    ],

    "rebalance": {
        "frequency": "monthly",
        "drift_threshold": 0.08,
        "force_if_position_above_max": True,
    },

    "evaluation_metrics": [
        "total_return",
        "max_drawdown",
        "cvar10",
        "sharpe",
        "sortino",
        "turnover",
    ],
}
```

## 3. Aggressive Growth

Formål:

```text
Maksimér upside/growth, accepter højere drawdown og koncentration.
```

Her kan strategy-laget tillade mere momentum og mindre cash.

```python
AGGRESSIVE_GROWTH = {
    "strategy_id": "aggressive_growth",
    "display_name": "Aggressive Growth",
    "risk_profile": "high",
    "objective": "upside_growth",

    "constraints": {
        "allow_shorting": False,
        "allow_margin": False,
        "max_position_weight": 0.35,
        "max_sector_weight": 0.65,
        "min_cash_weight": 0.00,
        "target_cash_weight": 0.03,
        "max_turnover_per_decision": 0.50,
    },

    "risk_policy": {
        "lambda_cvar": 0.30,
        "lambda_drawdown": 0.35,
        "lambda_volatility": 0.25,
        "lambda_transaction_cost": 0.25,
        "lambda_concentration": 0.30,
        "lambda_strategy_violation": 1.00,
        "score_quantile": "q75",
        "downside_metric": "cvar10",
    },

    "allowed_actions": [
        "HOLD",
        "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
        "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5",
        "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_10",
        "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_5",
        "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_10",
    ],

    "rebalance": {
        "frequency": "monthly",
        "drift_threshold": 0.12,
        "force_if_position_above_max": True,
    },

    "evaluation_metrics": [
        "total_return",
        "max_drawdown",
        "q90_return",
        "sharpe",
        "sortino",
        "turnover",
    ],
}
```

---

# Hvordan strategien bruges i DSS-score

Din IQN-agent leverer fx:

```text
q10, q25, q50, q75, q90, cvar10
```

for hver action.

Strategy-laget vælger så, hvordan disse skal scores.

Generel score:

[
Score(a)
========

## Q_\alpha(s,a)

## \lambda_{CVaR}|CVaR_{10}(s,a)|

## \lambda_{DD}DD(a)

## \lambda_C Cost(a)

## \lambda_K Concentration(a)

\lambda_S StrategyViolation(a)
]

Hvor (\alpha) afhænger af strategien:

```text
Defensive:  q50 eller q25
Balanced:   q50
Aggressive: q75
```

Så forskellen på strategierne er ikke kun UI-tekst. De ændrer faktisk beslutningslogikken.

---

# Eksempel: samme IQN-output, forskellig anbefaling

Antag IQN estimerer:

```text
Action                     q50     q75     cvar10
HOLD                       1.0%    2.0%    -2.5%
REBALANCE_TO_TARGETS       1.2%    2.1%    -1.8%
ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_10     2.0%    4.5%    -6.5%
INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET    0.4%    0.8%    -0.8%
```

Så kan systemet vælge:

```text
Defensive:
INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET eller REBALANCE_TO_TARGETS

Balanced:
REBALANCE_TO_TARGETS

Aggressive:
ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_10
```

Det er præcis den adfærd, du vil have.

---

# V2 action space koblet til strategy

Jeg ville definere et globalt action space:

```python
PORTFOLIO_ACTIONS = {
    0: "HOLD",
    1: "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
    2: "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
    3: "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25",
    4: "INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET",
    5: "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5",
    6: "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_10",
    7: "ADD_TO_LOWEST_RISK_5",
    8: "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_5",
    9: "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_10",
}
```

Men hver strategi må kun bruge nogle af dem.

Hvis IQN scorer en action, som strategien ikke tillader, gør du enten:

```text
A. masker action væk før selection
B. giver stor StrategyViolation penalty
```

Til PoC ville jeg bruge **masking** først:

```python
available_actions = [
    action for action in PORTFOLIO_ACTIONS
    if action in strategy["allowed_actions"]
]
```

Senere kan du bruge penalty, så systemet stadig kan forklare:

```text
ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_10 had high upside, but was rejected because it violates Defensive strategy constraints.
```

---

# Hvor strategy skal ligge i arkitekturen

Din V2-pipeline bliver:

```text
FinRL data pipeline
    ↓
FinRL-style portfolio environment
    ↓
Current portfolio state
    ↓
Investor strategy config
    ↓
Action generator / action mask
    ↓
IQN estimates distributions
    ↓
Risk policy scores actions
    ↓
Recommendation engine
    ↓
Audit log
```

Strategien bruges altså både før og efter IQN:

```text
Before IQN:
- hvilke actions er mulige/tilladte?
- hvilke constraints gælder?

After IQN:
- hvordan scores q10/q50/q90/CVaR?
- hvilken anbefaling gives?
- hvordan forklares beslutningen?
```

---

# Til rapporten: det originale bidrag

Det stærke ved dette er, at du kan skrive:

> FinRL provides the market environment and portfolio simulation foundation, while the proposed DSS introduces a strategy abstraction layer that maps investor preferences into action constraints, risk-aware scoring rules, and auditable recommendations.

På dansk:

> FinRL leverer fundamentet for markedsdata og porteføljesimulation, mens det foreslåede DSS introducerer et strategy abstraction layer, der oversætter investorens præferencer til handlingsbegrænsninger, risikojusteret scoring og auditerbare anbefalinger.

Det er et godt originalitetsargument.

---

# Hvad du bør implementere først

Lav en simpel fil:

```text
src/stockdss/strategies/predefined.py
```

med:

```python
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Literal


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyConfig:
    strategy_id: str
    display_name: str
    risk_profile: Literal["low", "medium", "high"]
    objective: str
    constraints: dict
    risk_policy: dict
    allowed_actions: list[str]
    rebalance: dict
    evaluation_metrics: list[str]


PREDEFINED_STRATEGIES = {
    "defensive_preservation": StrategyConfig(...),
    "balanced_growth": StrategyConfig(...),
    "aggressive_growth": StrategyConfig(...),
}


def get_strategy(strategy_id: str) -> StrategyConfig:
    try:
        return PREDEFINED_STRATEGIES[strategy_id]
    except KeyError as exc:
        available = ", ".join(PREDEFINED_STRATEGIES)
        raise ValueError(
            f"Unknown strategy_id={strategy_id}. Available: {available}"
        ) from exc
```

Det er nok til V2.

---

# Skal `logs/` være under `outputs/`?

Min anbefaling:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/
```

bør være det primære sted for eksperiment-logs.

Top-level:

```text
logs/
```

kan godt eksistere, men kun til generelle runtime/dev logs.

Så i praksis:

```text
outputs/
└─ runs/
   └─ 2026_05_17_1430_v2_smoke_test/
      ├─ config/
      ├─ data/
      ├─ models/
      ├─ logs/
      ├─ audit/
      ├─ plots/
      ├─ metrics/
      └─ summary/
```

Det er bedst, fordi hver run-folder bliver selvstændig og reproducerbar.

Så ja:

> **Eksperiment-logs skal ligge under outputs/runs/run_id/logs.**

Top-level `logs/` er kun praktisk fallback.

---

# V2 run output struktur

Hver gang du kører en runner, bør den oprette:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/
│
├─ config/
│  ├─ preset.yaml
│  ├─ strategy.json
│  ├─ universe.json
│  └─ iqn_config.json
│
├─ data/
│  ├─ train_data.csv
│  ├─ validation_data.csv
│  ├─ simulation_data.csv
│  └─ scaler.json
│
├─ models/
│  └─ iqn_model.pt
│
├─ logs/
│  ├─ run.log
│  └─ training.log
│
├─ audit/
│  ├─ decision_log.csv
│  ├─ recommendation_log.csv
│  └─ model_card.json
│
├─ metrics/
│  ├─ portfolio_metrics.csv
│  ├─ action_metrics.csv
│  └─ baseline_comparison.csv
│
├─ plots/
│  ├─ portfolio_value.png
│  ├─ drawdown.png
│  ├─ action_scores_last_decision.png
│  ├─ quantile_functions_last_decision.png
│  └─ baseline_comparison.png
│
└─ summary/
   ├─ run_summary.md
   └─ run_summary.json
```

Det er meget bedre end at have plots, logs, models og csv spredt ud over projektet.

---

# Hvad skal i `experiments/`?

`experiments/` skal ikke indeholde resultater.

Den skal indeholde **input-konfigurationer**.

Altså:

```text
experiments = what should be run
outputs     = what happened when it ran
```

Eksempel:

```yaml
# experiments/presets/recent_live_like_2025_2026.yaml

preset_id: recent_live_like_2025_2026

train:
  start: "2017-01-01"
  end: "2023-12-31"

validation:
  start: "2024-01-01"
  end: "2024-12-31"

simulation:
  start: "2025-01-01"
  end: "2026-05-17"
  decision_frequency: "weekly"

initial_capital: 1000000
strategy_id: balanced_growth
universe_id: universe_tech_10
```

---

# Hvad skal vi bygge først?

Ja, arbejdsplanen bør følge pipeline’en, men som en **thin vertical slice**.

Ikke sådan her:

```text
Byg hele data layer perfekt
Byg hele env perfekt
Byg hele strategy builder perfekt
...
```

Men sådan her:

```text
Lav minimal data → minimal env → minimal strategy → minimal IQN → minimal run
```

Målet er, at du hurtigt kan køre:

```powershell
python -m stockdss.runner.run_v2_smoke_test
```

og få:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/
```

med en komplet, men simpel, V2-run.

---

# Arbejdsplan V2 indenfor et par timer

## Step 1 — paths + run folder

Først:

```text
src/stockdss/utils/paths.py
src/stockdss/utils/logging.py
```

Formål:

```text
create_run_dir()
save_config_snapshot()
setup_logger()
```

Output:

```text
outputs/runs/2026_05_17_XXXX_v2_smoke_test/
```

Det er vigtigt, fordi alt andet skal skrive pænt ned i én run-folder.

---

## Step 2 — predefined strategies

Lav:

```text
src/stockdss/strategies/predefined.py
```

med:

```text
defensive_preservation
balanced_growth
aggressive_growth
```

Ingen strategy builder endnu.

Kun hardcoded configs.

---

## Step 3 — global portfolio actions

Lav:

```text
src/stockdss/envs/action_mapper.py
src/stockdss/dss/action_generator.py
```

Start med 6 actions, ikke 10:

```text
0 HOLD
1 REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS
2 REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10
3 REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25
4 INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET
5 ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5
```

Det er nok til V2 smoke test.

---

## Step 4 — minimal data pipeline

Lav:

```text
src/stockdss/data/finrl_data_pipeline.py
src/stockdss/data/pit_splits.py
src/stockdss/data/feature_scaler.py
```

Målet er ikke perfekt FinRL-integration endnu.

Målet er:

```text
load price data
filter universe
split train/validation/simulation
fit scaler on train only
apply scaler to validation/simulation
```

Hvis FinRL data processor virker nu, brug den. Hvis ikke, brug dine eksisterende CSV’er som fallback, men navngiv modulet stadig `finrl_data_pipeline.py`.

---

## Step 5 — minimal portfolio env

Lav:

```text
src/stockdss/envs/discrete_portfolio_dss_env.py
src/stockdss/envs/portfolio_accounting.py
src/stockdss/envs/reward.py
```

Dette er V2’s kerne.

Den skal kunne:

```text
reset()
step(discrete_action)
get_current_state()
get_portfolio_value()
```

Og state skal mindst indeholde:

```text
prices/features for universe
cash
holdings
weights
portfolio value
current drawdown
strategy id encoded
```

---

## Step 6 — IQN reuse

Flyt/genbrug din eksisterende IQN:

```text
src/stockdss/rl/iqn/agent.py
src/stockdss/rl/iqn/network.py
src/stockdss/rl/iqn/replay_buffer.py
src/stockdss/rl/iqn/trainer.py
```

Du skal ikke perfektionere den nu.

Få den til at acceptere:

```text
state_dim
num_actions
```

og træne på den nye env.

---

## Step 7 — risk policy + recommendation

Lav:

```text
src/stockdss/dss/risk_policy.py
src/stockdss/dss/recommendation_engine.py
```

Minimal score:

[
Score(a) = q50(a) - \lambda \cdot |CVaR10(a)|
]

Hvor (\lambda) kommer fra strategy config.

Det er nok.

---

## Step 8 — audit log

Lav:

```text
src/stockdss/dss/audit_log.py
```

Den skal skrive:

```text
decision_date
strategy_id
portfolio_value_before
selected_action
q10
q50
q90
cvar10
risk_adjusted_score
portfolio_value_after
```

til:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/audit/decision_log.csv
```

---

## Step 9 — runner

Lav:

```text
src/stockdss/runner/run_v2_smoke_test.py
```

Den skal gøre alt:

```text
1. create run folder
2. load config/preset
3. load data
4. split PIT
5. load strategy
6. create env
7. train IQN
8. simulate PIT
9. write audit
10. create plots/summary
```

Det er den vigtigste fil for dig lige nu.

---

# Minimal V2 runner flow

```python
def main():
    run_dir = create_run_dir("v2_smoke_test")

    preset = load_preset("recent_live_like_2025_2026")
    strategy = get_strategy("balanced_growth")

    dataset = load_finrl_dataset_or_csv(
        universe=preset.universe,
        start=preset.train.start,
        end=preset.simulation.end,
    )

    train_df, val_df, sim_df = make_pit_splits(dataset, preset)

    scaler = fit_scaler(train_df)
    train_df = apply_scaler(train_df, scaler)
    val_df = apply_scaler(val_df, scaler)
    sim_df = apply_scaler(sim_df, scaler)

    env_train = DiscretePortfolioDssEnv(
        data=train_df,
        strategy=strategy,
        initial_capital=preset.initial_capital,
    )

    agent = IQNAgent(
        state_dim=env_train.state_dim,
        num_actions=env_train.action_space.n,
    )

    train_iqn(agent, env_train)

    env_sim = DiscretePortfolioDssEnv(
        data=sim_df,
        strategy=strategy,
        initial_capital=preset.initial_capital,
    )

    simulate_with_audit(
        agent=agent,
        env=env_sim,
        strategy=strategy,
        run_dir=run_dir,
    )

    summarize_run(run_dir)
```

Det er præcis den vertikale slice, du skal ramme.

---

# Skal vi starte fra toppen af pipeline’en?

Ja — men med denne rækkefølge:

```text
1. run folder / paths
2. strategy configs
3. actions
4. data split
5. env
6. IQN
7. risk policy
8. recommendation
9. audit
10. plots/summary
```

Det svarer til pipeline’en, men i en implementerbar rækkefølge.

---

# Hvad skal ikke med i V2 første par timer?

Drop foreløbig:

```text
strategy builder UI
custom user-created JSON strategies
live broker integration
real user login
dynamic universe
sector classification
full FinRL baseline grid
Docker
k3s
database write layer
advanced model registry
online retraining
```

Det kommer senere.

Lige nu skal du have:

```text
hardcoded strategy
fixed universe
fixed preset
frozen/simple model
PIT simulation
audit log
plots
summary
```

---

# Den vigtigste V2-definition

Din V2 bør defineres sådan:

```text
V2 = FinRL-centered multi-asset, strategy-aware, discrete-action IQN-DSS prototype.
```

Minimum:

```text
Input:
- universe
- PIT preset
- initial capital
- strategy_id

Process:
- load/split data
- train IQN
- simulate portfolio decisions
- score actions using strategy risk policy
- log decisions

Output:
- portfolio history
- action log
- recommendation log
- risk metrics
- plots
```

---

# Den helt konkrete næste arbejdsplan

Hvis du vil ramme noget brugbart hurtigt, så gør dette i denne rækkefølge:

```text
A. Opret folder structure
B. Flyt gammel AAPL-IQN til legacy/
C. Lav predefined.py med 3 strategier
D. Lav action_mapper.py med 6 actions
E. Lav discrete_portfolio_dss_env.py med minimal accounting
F. Genbrug IQNAgent
G. Lav run_v2_smoke_test.py
H. Få ét run til at skrive outputs/runs/<run_id>/
```

Først når det virker, udvider du med mere FinRL-baseline og pænere plots.

---

# Kort svar

Ja:

> `runner/`, `experiments/`, `outputs/` og logs bør være med.

Men:

```text
runner/      = Python entrypoints under src/stockdss/runner/
experiments/ = config/presets/input
outputs/     = generated run artifacts
logs/        = mostly inside outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/
```

Og ja:

> Arbejdsplanen bør følge pipeline’en oppefra og ned, men som en tynd vertikal slice, så du hurtigt får et fuldt kørende V2-system.

Den vigtigste sætning for de næste par timer:

```text
Ikke perfekt arkitektur først — runnable V2 pipeline først.
```

# Hvad skal i top-level `logs/`?

Top-level `logs/` skal bruges til ting som:

```text
FinRL download fejlede
Yahoo/yfinance/FinRL API error
Python exception før run_dir blev oprettet
config kunne ikke læses
manglende dependency
import error
CUDA/torch error
unexpected crash
```

Eksempel:

```text
logs/system.log
```

```text
2026-05-17 15:22:10 INFO  Starting StockDSS V2 smoke test
2026-05-17 15:22:11 INFO  Loading preset recent_live_like_2025_2026
2026-05-17 15:22:15 ERROR FinRL data download failed for ticker NVDA
```

Og:

```text
logs/errors.log
```

```text
2026-05-17 15:22:15 ERROR ValueError: Missing required column 'tic' in processed dataframe
```

Det er altså debugging-logs.

---

# Hvad skal i `outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/`?

Det er logs for et bestemt run.

Eksempel:

```text
outputs/runs/2026_05_17_1530_v2_smoke_test/logs/run.log
```

```text
Run id: 2026_05_17_1530_v2_smoke_test
Preset: recent_live_like_2025_2026
Strategy: balanced_growth
Universe: tech_10
Initial capital: 1000000
Train period: 2017-2023
Validation period: 2024
Simulation period: 2025-2026
```

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/training.log
```

```text
Episode 1 reward ...
Episode 2 reward ...
Loss ...
Epsilon ...
```

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/backtest.log
```

```text
2025-01-03 action=HOLD portfolio_value=...
2025-01-10 action=REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS portfolio_value=...
```

Så run-logs er en del af det reproducerbare output.

---

# Derfor bør `utils/logging.py` understøtte begge

Du skal have én logging utility, der kan logge til:

```text
logs/system.log
```

og, når et run er oprettet:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/run.log
```

Minimal struktur:

```text
src/stockdss/utils/
  logging.py
  paths.py
```

## `paths.py`

```python
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime


PROJECT_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[3]

LOGS_DIR = PROJECT_ROOT / "logs"
OUTPUTS_DIR = PROJECT_ROOT / "outputs"
RUNS_DIR = OUTPUTS_DIR / "runs"


def ensure_base_dirs() -> None:
    LOGS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    RUNS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)


def create_run_dir(name: str) -> Path:
    ensure_base_dirs()

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y_%m_%d_%H%M")
    run_id = f"{timestamp}_{name}"

    run_dir = RUNS_DIR / run_id

    for subdir in [
        "config",
        "data",
        "models",
        "logs",
        "audit",
        "metrics",
        "plots",
        "summary",
    ]:
        (run_dir / subdir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    return run_dir
```

## `logging.py`

```python
import logging
from pathlib import Path

from stockdss.utils.paths import LOGS_DIR


def setup_system_logger() -> logging.Logger:
    LOGS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    logger = logging.getLogger("stockdss.system")
    logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    logger.handlers.clear()

    formatter = logging.Formatter(
        "%(asctime)s | %(levelname)s | %(name)s | %(message)s"
    )

    system_file = logging.FileHandler(LOGS_DIR / "system.log", encoding="utf-8")
    system_file.setFormatter(formatter)
    system_file.setLevel(logging.INFO)

    error_file = logging.FileHandler(LOGS_DIR / "errors.log", encoding="utf-8")
    error_file.setFormatter(formatter)
    error_file.setLevel(logging.ERROR)

    console = logging.StreamHandler()
    console.setFormatter(formatter)
    console.setLevel(logging.INFO)

    logger.addHandler(system_file)
    logger.addHandler(error_file)
    logger.addHandler(console)

    return logger


def setup_run_logger(run_dir: Path) -> logging.Logger:
    log_dir = run_dir / "logs"
    log_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    logger = logging.getLogger("stockdss.run")
    logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    logger.handlers.clear()

    formatter = logging.Formatter(
        "%(asctime)s | %(levelname)s | %(name)s | %(message)s"
    )

    run_file = logging.FileHandler(log_dir / "run.log", encoding="utf-8")
    run_file.setFormatter(formatter)
    run_file.setLevel(logging.INFO)

    error_file = logging.FileHandler(log_dir / "errors.log", encoding="utf-8")
    error_file.setFormatter(formatter)
    error_file.setLevel(logging.ERROR)

    console = logging.StreamHandler()
    console.setFormatter(formatter)
    console.setLevel(logging.INFO)

    logger.addHandler(run_file)
    logger.addHandler(error_file)
    logger.addHandler(console)

    return logger
```

---

# Praktisk brug i runner

I `run_v2_smoke_test.py`:

```python
from stockdss.utils.paths import create_run_dir
from stockdss.utils.logging import setup_system_logger, setup_run_logger


def main():
    system_logger = setup_system_logger()
    system_logger.info("Starting StockDSS V2 smoke test")

    try:
        run_dir = create_run_dir("v2_smoke_test")
        run_logger = setup_run_logger(run_dir)

        run_logger.info("Run directory created: %s", run_dir)

        # resten af pipeline
        # load data
        # train
        # simulate
        # save outputs

    except Exception:
        system_logger.exception("V2 smoke test failed before completion")
        raise


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

Så hvis noget crasher, får du det i:

```text
logs/errors.log
```

og hvis run-dir allerede var oprettet, kan du også logge det i:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/errors.log
```

# Justeret project structure

Så jeg ville opdatere strukturen sådan her:

```text
StockInvestmentDSS/
│
├─ logs/
│  ├─ system.log              # generel system/debug log
│  ├─ errors.log              # globale Python/errors
│  └─ data_pipeline.log       # optional: data download/cache/debug
│
├─ outputs/
│  └─ runs/
│     └─ <run_id>/
│        ├─ logs/
│        │  ├─ run.log
│        │  ├─ errors.log
│        │  ├─ training.log
│        │  └─ simulation.log
│        ├─ plots/
│        ├─ models/
│        ├─ metrics/
│        ├─ audit/
│        ├─ config/
│        └─ summary/
│
└─ src/
   └─ stockdss/
      └─ utils/
         ├─ paths.py
         └─ logging.py
```

---

# Kort regel

```text
logs/
= system/debugging på tværs af runs

outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/
= logs der hører til ét konkret run
```

Så ja: **du havde ret**. Der bør være en top-level `logs/` til systemfejl, data pipeline failures og Python exceptions, mens alle run-specifikke artifacts bliver samlet under `outputs/runs/<run_id>/`.

ChatGPT:

Ja — **ObjectRL_Clean-vejen er fin som reference**, men jeg ville **ikke kopiere hele ObjectRL_Clean ind som startpunkt**.

Jeg ville gøre sådan:

```text
FinRL_IQN/
  = ny V2-mappe, ren struktur

ObjectRL_Clean/
  = reference/kilde til IQN-implementationen

ObjectRL_style/
  = legacy V1 / eksperimentelt AAPL-system
```

Din `FinRL_IQN` mappe er allerede tom, og det er faktisk perfekt som V2-startpunkt. 

Så: **start rent i `FinRL_IQN`**, men kopier/genbrug selektivt fra `ObjectRL_Clean/IQN/src/stockdss/rl/...`.

---

# Min anbefaling

Du bør ikke starte med:

```text
Copy ObjectRL_Clean → FinRL_IQN
```

fordi ObjectRL_Clean stadig er organiseret omkring:

```text
IQN først
environment bagefter
```

Men V2 skal være:

```text
FinRL data/environment først
IQN ovenpå
DSS/risk/audit bagefter
```

Så vi skal bygge V2-mappen sådan, at arkitekturen allerede fortæller den rigtige historie.

---

# Aftalt V2-mappe

I din eksisterende struktur:

```text
D-IQN-DSS/
│
├─ ObjectRL_style/       # legacy V1 / eksperimentel AAPL prototype
├─ ObjectRL_Clean/       # ren IQN reference
├─ FinRL_IQN/            # ny V2
```

`FinRL_IQN/` skal være den nye hovedmappe.

# Hvad kopierer vi fra ObjectRL_Clean?

Kun IQN-kernen.

Fra `ObjectRL_Clean/IQN/src/stockdss/rl/...` kopierer vi sandsynligvis:

```text
agent
network / net
replay buffer
quantile loss
trainer-idéer
config-idéer
```

Men vi flytter det ind i ny struktur:

```text
FinRL_IQN/src/stockdss/rl/iqn/
```

Så vi får:

```text
ObjectRL_Clean:
  reference implementation

FinRL_IQN:
  production-ish V2 implementation
```

Det er bedre end at lade gammel struktur styre ny arkitektur.

---

# Hvad skal ikke kopieres?

Jeg ville ikke kopiere:

```text
gamle single-stock envs
gamle AAPL-runners
gamle output-path conventions
gamle experiment folders
gamle plots/results/trained_models-struktur
```

De ting skabte netop den V1-kompleksitet, vi prøver at slippe ud af.

---

# V2 arbejdsplan — ja, vi starter oppefra

Ja, din pipeline skal være arbejdsplanen:

```text
FinRL data pipeline
↓
FinRL-style portfolio environment
↓
Current portfolio state
↓
Investor strategy config
↓
Action generator / action mask
↓
IQN estimates distributions
↓
Risk policy scores actions
↓
Recommendation engine
↓
Audit log
```

Men vi bygger den som en **thin vertical slice**:

## Første mål

Ikke “perfekt FinRL-system”.

Første mål er:

```text
python -m stockdss.runner.run_v2_smoke_test
```

og at den opretter:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/
├─ logs/
├─ audit/
├─ metrics/
├─ plots/
├─ models/
├─ config/
└─ summary/
```

---

# V2 build-order

## Step 0 — create structure

Først laver du mappestrukturen i `FinRL_IQN`.

## Step 1 — utilities

```text
utils/paths.py
utils/logging.py
utils/config.py
utils/seed.py
```

Fordi alt andet skal kunne:

```text
create_run_dir()
log system errors
log run errors
load yaml config
set seed
```

## Step 2 — predefined strategies

```text
strategies/predefined.py
strategies/constraints.py
```

Hardcoded:

```text
defensive_preservation
balanced_growth
aggressive_growth
```

## Step 3 — actions

```text
envs/action_mapper.py
dss/action_generator.py
```

Start med 6 actions:

```text
HOLD
REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS
REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10
REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25
INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET
ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5
```

## Step 4 — FinRL data pipeline

```text
data/finrl_data_pipeline.py
data/pit_splits.py
data/feature_scaler.py
```

Her skal FinRL bruges så centralt som muligt:

```text
FinRL/YahooDownloader eller lokal cache
FinRL FeatureEngineer hvor muligt
FinRL-format: date, tic, open, high, low, close, volume, indicators
```

Hvis download fejler, logger vi til:

```text
logs/data_pipeline.log
logs/errors.log
```

og falder tilbage til cache, hvis den findes.

## Step 5 — portfolio env

```text
envs/discrete_portfolio_dss_env.py
envs/portfolio_accounting.py
envs/reward.py
```

Denne skal bruge FinRL-style dataframe, men have discrete actions.

## Step 6 — IQN

```text
rl/iqn/
```

Her genbruger vi fra ObjectRL_Clean.

## Step 7 — DSS

```text
dss/risk_policy.py
dss/recommendation_engine.py
dss/audit_log.py
```

Minimal scoring:

```text
score = q50 - lambda_cvar * abs(cvar10)
```

## Step 8 — runner

```text
runner/run_v2_smoke_test.py
```

Den binder alt sammen.

---

# ObjectRL_Clean er fin — men kun som donor

Så svaret på dit spørgsmål er:

> Ja, ObjectRL_Clean-vejen er fin, men ikke som mappebase. Den er fin som donor for IQN-implementationen.

Den nye V2 skal være `FinRL_IQN`, fordi navnet og strukturen skal vise:

```text
FinRL først
IQN ovenpå
DSS som beslutningslag
```

---

# Konkret beslutning

Vi aftaler:

```text
D-IQN-DSS/FinRL_IQN/
```

bliver V2.

Vi efterlader:

```text
ObjectRL_style/
ObjectRL_Clean/
```

urørt.

Vi kopierer kun nødvendige IQN-filer ind senere.

Den første fil du bør lave er ikke IQN-agenten.

Det er:

```text
scripts/create_structure.ps1
```

eller manuelt oprette strukturen.

Derefter:

```text
src/stockdss/utils/paths.py
src/stockdss/utils/logging.py
src/stockdss/strategies/predefined.py
src/stockdss/envs/action_mapper.py
```

Så har vi fundamentet for V2.

---

# Den korte version

Ja:

```text
ObjectRL_Clean = god reference
FinRL_IQN = korrekt V2-start
```

Nej:

```text
Kopier ikke hele ObjectRL_Clean ukritisk ind.
```

Gør i stedet:

```text
1. Start tomt i FinRL_IQN
2. Opret V2-struktur
3. Brug FinRL centralt fra data/environment-siden
4. Kopier kun IQN-kernen fra ObjectRL_Clean
5. Byg pipeline top-down som thin vertical slice
```

Det er den hurtigste vej til en brugbar V2 indenfor få timer.

ChatGPT:

Ja — jeg ville stadig lave `scripts/create_structure.ps1`, selvom du allerede har lavet meget manuelt.

Grunden er enkel: scriptet bliver **idempotent dokumentation** af V2-strukturen. Du kan køre det igen uden at ødelægge noget, og det opretter kun manglende mapper/filer.

Din nuværende manuelle struktur er fin som start:

```text
FinRL_IQN/
├── data
├── experiments
├── logs
├── outputs/runs
└── src
    ├── data
    ├── dss
    ├── environments
    ├── rl
    ├── runner
    ├── strategies
    └── utilities
```

Men jeg vil klart anbefale én ændring:

```text
src/
└── stockdss/
```

I stedet for direkte:

```text
src/data
src/dss
src/environments
...
```

Ellers bliver det irriterende at køre:

```powershell
python -m stockdss.runner.run_v2_smoke_test
```

Så den rigtige V2-struktur bør være:

```text
src/
└── stockdss/
    ├── data
    ├── dss
    ├── environments
    ├── reinforcement_learning
    ├── runner
    ├── strategies
    └── utilities
```

Her er scriptet.

```powershell
# scripts/create_structure.ps1
# Creates the StockDSS FinRL-IQN V2 project structure.
# Safe to run multiple times.

$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"

Write-Host "Creating FinRL-IQN V2 project structure..." -ForegroundColor Cyan

# Resolve project root as the parent folder of /scripts.
$ScriptDirectory = Split-Path -Parent $MyInvocation.MyCommand.Path
$ProjectRoot = Split-Path -Parent $ScriptDirectory

Set-Location $ProjectRoot

function New-DirectoryIfMissing {
    param (
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Path
    )

    if (-not (Test-Path $Path)) {
        New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $Path | Out-Null
        Write-Host "Created directory: $Path" -ForegroundColor Green
    }
}

function New-FileIfMissing {
    param (
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Path,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [string] $Content = ""
    )

    if (-not (Test-Path $Path)) {
        $Parent = Split-Path -Parent $Path

        if ($Parent -and -not (Test-Path $Parent)) {
            New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $Parent | Out-Null
        }

        Set-Content -Path $Path -Value $Content -Encoding UTF8
        Write-Host "Created file: $Path" -ForegroundColor Green
    }
}

# Top-level directories
$Directories = @(
    "data",
    "data\raw",
    "data\processed",
    "data\cache",

    "experiments",
    "experiments\presets",
    "experiments\universes",
    "experiments\configs",

    "logs",

    "outputs",
    "outputs\runs",

    "scripts",

    "src",
    "src\stockdss",

    "src\stockdss\data",
    "src\stockdss\dss",
    "src\stockdss\environments",
    "src\stockdss\strategies",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\iqn",
    "src\stockdss\baselines",
    "src\stockdss\evaluation",
    "src\stockdss\runner",
    "src\stockdss\utilities"
)

foreach ($Directory in $Directories) {
    New-DirectoryIfMissing $Directory
}

# Python package marker files
$PythonInitFiles = @(
    "src\stockdss\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\data\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\dss\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\environments\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\strategies\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\iqn\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\baselines\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\evaluation\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\runner\__init__.py",
    "src\stockdss\utilities\__init__.py"
)

foreach ($File in $PythonInitFiles) {
    New-FileIfMissing $File
}

# Keep empty folders in Git
$GitKeepFiles = @(
    "data\raw\.gitkeep",
    "data\processed\.gitkeep",
    "data\cache\.gitkeep",
    "logs\.gitkeep",
    "outputs\runs\.gitkeep"
)

foreach ($File in $GitKeepFiles) {
    New-FileIfMissing $File
}

# Core source files
$SourceFiles = @(
    "src\stockdss\data\finrl_data_pipeline.py",
    "src\stockdss\data\point_in_time_splits.py",
    "src\stockdss\data\feature_scaler.py",
    "src\stockdss\data\market_dataset.py",

    "src\stockdss\environments\discrete_portfolio_decision_support_environment.py",
    "src\stockdss\environments\portfolio_accounting.py",
    "src\stockdss\environments\action_mapper.py",
    "src\stockdss\environments\reward.py",

    "src\stockdss\strategies\predefined.py",
    "src\stockdss\strategies\constraints.py",

    "src\stockdss\dss\action_generator.py",
    "src\stockdss\dss\risk_policy.py",
    "src\stockdss\dss\recommendation_engine.py",
    "src\stockdss\dss\audit_log.py",

    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\iqn\agent.py",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\iqn\network.py",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\iqn\replay_buffer.py",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\iqn\trainer.py",
    "src\stockdss\reinforcement_learning\iqn\quantile_loss.py",

    "src\stockdss\baselines\equal_weight.py",
    "src\stockdss\baselines\buy_and_hold.py",
    "src\stockdss\baselines\mean_variance_optimization.py",
    "src\stockdss\baselines\finrl_baselines.py",

    "src\stockdss\evaluation\metrics.py",

    "src\stockdss\evaluation\summarize.py",

    "src\stockdss\runner\run_v2_smoke_test.py",
    "src\stockdss\runner\train_iqn_portfolio.py",
    "src\stockdss\runner\simulate_point_in_time_decision_support.py",

    "src\stockdss\utilities\paths.py",
    "src\stockdss\utilities\logging.py",
    "src\stockdss\utilities\configuration.py",
    "src\stockdss\utilities\seed.py"
)

foreach ($File in $SourceFiles) {
    New-FileIfMissing $File
}

# Experiment input files
New-FileIfMissing "experiments\presets\recent_live_like_2025_2026.yaml" @"
```

## Hvad du skal gøre nu

Gem scriptet her:

```text
FinRL_IQN/scripts/create_structure.ps1
```

Kør fra `FinRL_IQN`:

```powershell
.\scripts\create_structure.ps1
```

Efter det bør `tree` vise cirka:

```text
FinRL_IQN/
├── data
├── experiments
├── logs
├── outputs
├── scripts
└── src
    └── stockdss
        ├── baselines
        ├── data
        ├── dss
        ├── environments
        ├── evaluation
        ├── reinforcement_learning
        ├── runner
        ├── strategies
        └── utilities
```

Jeg ville bruge scriptet og lade det tilføje `src/stockdss/...` ovenpå din manuelle struktur. Den gamle direkte `src/data`, `src/dss`, osv. kan du enten lade ligge tomt midlertidigt eller slette dem bagefter. For V2 bør vi arbejde i `src/stockdss/...`.

```text
    └── utilities
```

Den er fin. Vi bruger den.

Og ja: V2 skal være grundlaget for det senere webbaserede PoC-produkt. Derfor er det vigtigere, at flowet virker, end at mappestrukturen er perfekt akademisk fra start.

## Aftale for V2

Vi arbejder videre i:

```text
D-IQN-DSS/FinRL_IQN/
```

Vi efterlader:

```text
ObjectRL_style/
ObjectRL_Clean/
```

urørt.

Og vi bygger kun de filer, vi faktisk skal bruge.

---

# Minimal V2-struktur nu

Jeg ville justere din nuværende struktur sådan her, men uden at overbygge den:

```text
FinRL_IQN/
├── data/
│   ├── raw/
│   ├── processed/
│   └── cache/
│
├── experiments/
│   ├── presets/
│   ├── universes/
│   └── configs/
│
├── logs/
│   ├── system.log
│   ├── errors.log
│   └── data_pipeline.log
│
├── outputs/
│   └── runs/
│
└── src/
    ├── data/
    ├── environments/
    ├── strategies/
    ├── dss/
    ├── rl/
    ├── runner/
    └── utilities/
```

Ingen `stockdss` package lige nu, hvis du foretrækker at holde det enkelt. Så kører vi i stedet med:

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH="src"
python .\src\runner\run_v2_smoke_test.py
```

Det er helt fint til PoC.

Senere kan vi pakke det pænere ind som:

```text
src/stockdss/...
```

men det behøver vi ikke nu.

# Kun de første nødvendige filer

Vi starter med **8–10 filer**, ikke 50.

```text
src/
├── utilities/
│   ├── paths.py
│   └── logging_setup.py
│
├── strategies/
│   └── predefined_strategies.py
│
├── environments/
│   ├── portfolio_actions.py
│   └── portfolio_accounting.py

│   └── finrl_data_pipeline.py

├── dss/
│   ├── risk_policy.py
│   └── audit_log.py
│
└── runner/
    └── run_v2_smoke_test.py
```

Det er nok til at komme i gang.

Derefter tilføjer vi IQN-filer fra `ObjectRL_Clean`, men først når data/env/strategy-flowet kører.

---

# V2 arbejdsplan

Ja, vi følger pipeline’en:

```text
FinRL data pipeline
↓
FinRL-style portfolio environment
↓
Current portfolio state
↓
Investor strategy config
↓
Action generator / action mask
↓
IQN estimates distributions
↓
Risk policy scores actions
↓
Recommendation engine
↓
Audit log
```

Men første delmål er ikke IQN-træning endnu.

Første delmål er:

```text
FinRL data → portfolio state → strategy → actions → dummy recommendation → audit log
```

Altså en **DSS smoke test uden IQN først**.

Det er vigtigt, fordi så ved vi, at produkt-flowet virker.

Derefter sætter vi IQN ind i midten.

---

# Rækkefølge for de næste filer

## 1. `utilities/paths.py`

Ansvar:

```text
find project root
create run folder
create run subfolders
```

## 2. `utilities/logging_setup.py`

Ansvar:

```text
system/debug logs til logs/
run logs til outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/
```

## 3. `strategies/predefined_strategies.py`

Ansvar:

```text
defensive_preservation
balanced_growth
aggressive_growth
```

## 4. `environments/portfolio_actions.py`

Ansvar:

```text
HOLD
REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS
REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10
REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25
INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET
ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5
```

## 5. `data/finrl_data_pipeline.py`

Ansvar:

```text
hent/load data via FinRL/yfinance/cache
returner dataframe i FinRL-format
```

## 6. `runner/run_v2_smoke_test.py`

Ansvar:

```text
kør hele flowet minimalt
opret run folder
load strategy
load data
lav dummy portfolio
lav dummy recommendation
skriv audit log
```

Når det virker, går vi videre til:

```text
IQN agent
IQN network
replay buffer
trainer
simulation environment
```

Vi tilføjer kun filer, når vi faktisk skal bruge dem.

V2-målet er:

```text
Et kørende FinRL-IQN-DSS prototype-flow, der kan danne grundlag for det senere webbaserede PoC-produkt.
```

Første rigtige milepæl:

skal oprette:

og bevise:


Derefter sætter vi IQN ind.

ChatGPT:

Ja, det giver mening at tilføje **Weights & Biases**, men jeg ville gøre det som **valgfri integration**, ikke som noget hele V2 afhænger af.

Altså:

```text
V2 skal kunne køre uden W&B.
Hvis W&B er slået til, logger vi metrics dér også.
```

Det er vigtigt, fordi du ikke vil have, at hele pipeline fejler, bare fordi W&B-token mangler eller internettet driller.

Din nuværende struktur ser god ud:

```text
src/stockdss/utilities/
├── config.py
├── logging.py
├── paths.py
└── seed.py
```

Jeg ville tilføje én fil:

```text
src/stockdss/utilities/experiment_tracking.py
```

Ikke kalde den `wandb.py`, fordi det kan konflikte med selve `wandb`-pakken.

Så:

```text
src/stockdss/utilities/
├── config.py
├── experiment_tracking.py
├── logging.py
├── paths.py
└── seed.py
```

## Rollen for `experiment_tracking.py`

Den skal håndtere:

```text
- start W&B run, hvis enabled
- log metrics, hvis enabled
- log config, hvis enabled
- luk run pænt
- gøre ingenting, hvis W&B er disabled
```

Minimal idé:

```python
# src/stockdss/utilities/experiment_tracking.py

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Any


@dataclass
class ExperimentTracker:
    enabled: bool = False
    project_name: str = "stockdss-finrl-iqn"
    run_name: str | None = None
    _wandb_run: Any = None

    def start(self, config: dict[str, Any] | None = None) -> None:
        if not self.enabled:
            return

        try:
            import wandb
        except ImportError as exc:
            raise ImportError(
                "Weights & Biases is enabled, but the 'wandb' package is not installed."
            ) from exc

        self._wandb_run = wandb.init(
            project=self.project_name,
            name=self.run_name,
            config=config or {},
        )

    def log(self, metrics: dict[str, Any], step: int | None = None) -> None:
        if not self.enabled or self._wandb_run is None:
            return

        import wandb

        wandb.log(metrics, step=step)

    def finish(self) -> None:
        if not self.enabled or self._wandb_run is None:
            return

        import wandb

        wandb.finish()
        self._wandb_run = None
```

## I første omgang bør W&B være disabled som default

I `.env.example` eller config kan du have:

```text
STOCKDSS_USE_WANDB=false
STOCKDSS_WANDB_PROJECT=stockdss-finrl-iqn
```

Og i smoke testen:

```python
tracker = ExperimentTracker(
    enabled=False,
    project_name="stockdss-finrl-iqn",
    run_name=run_id,
)
```

Senere kan du slå det til.

## Hvad skal logges til W&B?

Til V2 ville jeg kun logge få ting:

```text
training/loss
training/episode_reward
portfolio/value
portfolio/total_return
portfolio/max_drawdown
portfolio/sharpe
actions/selected_action_id
risk/q10
risk/q50
risk/q90
risk/cvar10
risk/risk_adjusted_score
```

Men alle vigtige artifacts skal stadig gemmes lokalt i:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/
```

W&B er ekstra tracking — ikke source of truth.

## Kort beslutning

Ja, tilføj:

```text
src/stockdss/utilities/experiment_tracking.py
```

Men brug det først sådan:

```text
W&B optional
local outputs mandatory
system logs mandatory
run logs mandatory
```

Så V2 bliver robust, og du kan senere bruge W&B til at sammenligne IQN-runs, strategier og hyperparameters.

Me :

er det så i stockdss mappen at jeg placerer .env og .env.example?

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ChatGPT:

Nej — **ikke inde i `src/stockdss/`**.

Placér dem i **projektroden**:

```text
FinRL_IQN/
├── .env
├── .env.example
├── data/
├── experiments/
├── logs/
├── outputs/
└── src/
    └── stockdss/
        ├── data/
        ├── dss/
        ├── environments/
        ├── runner/
        ├── strategies/
        └── utilities/
```

Så altså her:

```text
C:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\DataScience\Speciale\D-IQN-DSS\FinRL_IQN\.env
C:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\DataScience\Speciale\D-IQN-DSS\FinRL_IQN\.env.example
```

Ikke her:

```text
FinRL_IQN/src/stockdss/.env
```

## Hvorfor?

Fordi `.env` er **projektkonfiguration**, ikke Python source code.

Den skal styre ting som:

```env
PYTHONPATH=src
STOCKDSS_LOG_LEVEL=INFO
STOCKDSS_USE_WANDB=false
STOCKDSS_WANDB_PROJECT=stockdss-finrl-iqn
STOCKDSS_DATA_SOURCE=finrl
STOCKDSS_CACHE_DIR=data/cache
STOCKDSS_OUTPUT_DIR=outputs/runs
```

## `.env.example` vs `.env`

Du tracker:

```text
.env.example
```

i Git.

Du ignorerer:

```text
.env
```

i `.gitignore`.

Så:

```gitignore
.env
.env.*
!.env.example
```

## Minimal `.env.example`

```env
PYTHONPATH=src

STOCKDSS_LOG_LEVEL=INFO

STOCKDSS_USE_WANDB=false
STOCKDSS_WANDB_PROJECT=stockdss-finrl-iqn

STOCKDSS_DATA_SOURCE=finrl
STOCKDSS_CACHE_DIR=data/cache
STOCKDSS_OUTPUT_DIR=outputs/runs

STOCKDSS_DEFAULT_PRESET=recent_live_like_2025_2026
STOCKDSS_DEFAULT_STRATEGY=balanced_growth
```

## Minimal `.env`

Du kan starte med samme indhold:

```env
PYTHONPATH=src
STOCKDSS_LOG_LEVEL=INFO

STOCKDSS_USE_WANDB=false
STOCKDSS_WANDB_PROJECT=stockdss-finrl-iqn

STOCKDSS_DATA_SOURCE=finrl
STOCKDSS_CACHE_DIR=data/cache
STOCKDSS_OUTPUT_DIR=outputs/runs

STOCKDSS_DEFAULT_PRESET=recent_live_like_2025_2026
STOCKDSS_DEFAULT_STRATEGY=balanced_growth
```

Senere, hvis du slår Weights & Biases til, kan du sætte:

```env
STOCKDSS_USE_WANDB=true
WANDB_API_KEY=...
```

men `WANDB_API_KEY` skal **kun** ligge i `.env`, aldrig i `.env.example`.

Kort regel:

```text
FinRL_IQN/.env          = lokal privat konfiguration
FinRL_IQN/.env.example  = offentlig template
src/stockdss/           = Python-kode
```

# Flyt ikke gammel `risk_policy.py` direkte med som hovedlogik

Din gamle:

```text

```

kan bruges som inspiration, men i V2 bør risk policy ligge her:

```text
src/stockdss/dss/risk_policy.py
```

Hvorfor?

Fordi risk policy ikke er selve RL-agenten.

Den er DSS-laget:

```text
IQN estimates distributions
↓
DSS risk policy scores actions
↓
Recommendation engine
```

Så `rl/` skal helst kun indeholde:

```text
agent
network
replay buffer
trainer
loss
config
```

Mens investorlogik ligger i:

```text
strategies/
dss/
environments/
```

---

# Vigtigt princip

IQN-agenten skal være **environment-agnostic**.

Den skal ikke vide noget om:

```text
AAPL
FinRL
portfolio
strategy
cash
rebalance
```

Den skal kun vide:

```text
state_dim
num_actions
state
action
reward
next_state
done
```

Det betyder:

```text
FinRL data pipeline
FinRL-style environment
portfolio state
strategy config
action mask
```

kommer udenfor `rl/`.

Og så bruger IQN bare det miljø, den får.

---

# Praktisk beslutning

Ja, kopier denne del ind:

```text
rl/agents/
rl/config/
rl/models/
rl/nets/
rl/replay_buffers/
rl/__init__.py
```

Vent med / undlad:

```text
rl/experiments/
rl/policies/
__pycache__/
```

---

# Hvis du vil kopiere manuelt

Fra din V1/clean mappe til V2:

```powershell
Copy-Item ..\ObjectRL_Clean\IQN\src\stockdss\rl\agents .\src\stockdss\rl\agents -Recurse
Copy-Item ..\ObjectRL_Clean\IQN\src\stockdss\rl\config .\src\stockdss\rl\config -Recurse
Copy-Item ..\ObjectRL_Clean\IQN\src\stockdss\rl\models .\src\stockdss\rl\models -Recurse
Copy-Item ..\ObjectRL_Clean\IQN\src\stockdss\rl\nets .\src\stockdss\rl\nets -Recurse
Copy-Item ..\ObjectRL_Clean\IQN\src\stockdss\rl\replay_buffers .\src\stockdss\rl\replay_buffers -Recurse
```

Derefter slet `__pycache__`:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem .\src\stockdss\rl -Recurse -Directory -Filter "__pycache__" | Remove-Item -Recurse -Force
```

# Konklusion

Ja:

```text
src/stockdss/rl/
```

kan være din nuværende IQN-implementation fra V1.

Men kun som **IQN engine**.

V2 skal ikke arve V1’s single-ticker experiments som aktiv struktur.

Den rigtige opdeling er:

```text
src/stockdss/data/          = FinRL data pipeline
src/stockdss/environments/  = FinRL-style portfolio environment
src/stockdss/strategies/    = predefined investor strategies
src/stockdss/dss/           = risk policy, recommendation, audit
src/stockdss/rl/            = IQN implementation
src/stockdss/runner/        = executable V2 workflows
```

Så ja: **genbrug IQN-kernen, men lad V2-arkitekturen styre resten.**

## 2. Fjern `__pycache__`

De er bare runtime-cache fra Python og skal ikke være i projektstrukturen.

Kør:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem .\src -Recurse -Directory -Filter "__pycache__" | Remove-Item -Recurse -Force
```

Og sørg for `.gitignore` har:

```gitignore
__pycache__/
*.pyc
```

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ChatGPT:

Ja — vi starter helt rigtigt med `utilities`, fordi **paths/logging/config/seed** er fundamentet for alt andet.

Og du har helt ret: i V1 blev det rodet, fordi flere dele selv fandt på output-stier. I V2 skal vi have én regel:

> **Ingen kode må selv opfinde output paths. Alt skal gå gennem `utilities.paths`.**

Så alle runners gør:

```python
run_paths = create_run_paths(run_name="v2_smoke_test")
```

og derefter skriver alt til:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/
```

---

## V2 path-princip

Vi bruger to typer stier:

```text
Project-level paths:
- logs/
- data/
- experiments/
- outputs/runs/

Run-level paths:
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/logs/
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/config/
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/data/
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/models/
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/plots/
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/audit/
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/metrics/
- outputs/runs/<run_id>/summary/
```

Så en runner får én `RunPaths`-object og sender den rundt. Ingen hardcoded `outputs/...` andre steder.

---

# 1. `src/stockdss/utilities/paths.py`

Indsæt dette:

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path


def find_project_root() -> Path:
    """
    Find the FinRL_IQN project root.

    Expected structure:
        FinRL_IQN/
            .env
            src/
                stockdss/
    """
    current_path = Path(__file__).resolve()

    for parent in current_path.parents:
        if (parent / "src").exists() and (parent / ".env.example").exists():
            return parent

    raise RuntimeError(
        "Could not find project root. Expected to find a folder containing "
        "'src/' and '.env.example'."
    )


PROJECT_ROOT = find_project_root()

DATA_DIRECTORY = PROJECT_ROOT / "data"
EXPERIMENTS_DIRECTORY = PROJECT_ROOT / "experiments"
LOGS_DIRECTORY = PROJECT_ROOT / "logs"
OUTPUTS_DIRECTORY = PROJECT_ROOT / "outputs"
RUNS_DIRECTORY = OUTPUTS_DIRECTORY / "runs"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class RunPaths:
    run_id: str
    run_directory: Path
    config_directory: Path
    data_directory: Path
    models_directory: Path
    logs_directory: Path
    audit_directory: Path
    metrics_directory: Path
    plots_directory: Path
    summary_directory: Path


def ensure_project_directories() -> None:
    """
    Create only the project-level directories.
    Safe to run repeatedly.
    """
    for directory in [
        DATA_DIRECTORY,
        EXPERIMENTS_DIRECTORY,
        LOGS_DIRECTORY,
        OUTPUTS_DIRECTORY,
        RUNS_DIRECTORY,
    ]:
        directory.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)


def create_run_paths(run_name: str) -> RunPaths:
    """
    Create a self-contained run directory under outputs/runs/.

    Example:
        outputs/runs/2026_05_17_0412_v2_smoke_test/
    """
    ensure_project_directories()

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y_%m_%d_%H%M%S")
    safe_run_name = run_name.strip().lower().replace(" ", "_")
    run_id = f"{timestamp}_{safe_run_name}"

    run_directory = RUNS_DIRECTORY / run_id

    config_directory = run_directory / "config"
    data_directory = run_directory / "data"
    models_directory = run_directory / "models"
    logs_directory = run_directory / "logs"
    audit_directory = run_directory / "audit"
    metrics_directory = run_directory / "metrics"
    plots_directory = run_directory / "plots"
    summary_directory = run_directory / "summary"

    for directory in [
        run_directory,
        config_directory,
        data_directory,
        models_directory,
        logs_directory,
        audit_directory,
        metrics_directory,
        plots_directory,
        summary_directory,
    ]:
        directory.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)

    return RunPaths(
        run_id=run_id,
        run_directory=run_directory,
        config_directory=config_directory,
        data_directory=data_directory,
        models_directory=models_directory,
        logs_directory=logs_directory,
        audit_directory=audit_directory,
        metrics_directory=metrics_directory,
        plots_directory=plots_directory,
        summary_directory=summary_directory,
    )
```

---

# 2. `src/stockdss/utilities/logging.py`

Indsæt dette:

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from pathlib import Path

from stockdss.utilities.paths import LOGS_DIRECTORY, RunPaths


LOG_FORMAT = "%(asctime)s | %(levelname)s | %(name)s | %(message)s"


def setup_system_logger(log_level: str = "INFO") -> logging.Logger:
    """
    System/debug logger.

    Used for:
    - startup errors
    - data pipeline failures
    - Python exceptions before a run exists
    """
    LOGS_DIRECTORY.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    logger = logging.getLogger("stockdss.system")
    logger.setLevel(log_level.upper())
    logger.handlers.clear()
    logger.propagate = False

    formatter = logging.Formatter(LOG_FORMAT)

    system_file_handler = logging.FileHandler(
        LOGS_DIRECTORY / "system.log",
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    system_file_handler.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    system_file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    error_file_handler = logging.FileHandler(
        LOGS_DIRECTORY / "errors.log",
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    error_file_handler.setLevel(logging.ERROR)
    error_file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
    console_handler.setLevel(log_level.upper())
    console_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    logger.addHandler(system_file_handler)
    logger.addHandler(error_file_handler)
    logger.addHandler(console_handler)

    return logger


def setup_run_logger(run_paths: RunPaths, log_level: str = "INFO") -> logging.Logger:
    """
    Run-specific logger.

    Used for:
    - one concrete training/simulation run
    - run.log
    - run-level errors.log
    """
    run_paths.logs_directory.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    logger = logging.getLogger(f"stockdss.run.{run_paths.run_id}")
    logger.setLevel(log_level.upper())
    logger.handlers.clear()
    logger.propagate = False

    formatter = logging.Formatter(LOG_FORMAT)

    run_file_handler = logging.FileHandler(
        run_paths.logs_directory / "run.log",
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    run_file_handler.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    run_file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    error_file_handler = logging.FileHandler(
        run_paths.logs_directory / "errors.log",
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    error_file_handler.setLevel(logging.ERROR)
    error_file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
    console_handler.setLevel(log_level.upper())
    console_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    logger.addHandler(run_file_handler)
    logger.addHandler(error_file_handler)
    logger.addHandler(console_handler)

    return logger


def setup_named_file_logger(
    logger_name: str,
    log_file: Path,
    log_level: str = "INFO",
) -> logging.Logger:
    """
    Optional logger for special cases, e.g. data_pipeline.log.
    """
    log_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    logger = logging.getLogger(logger_name)
    logger.setLevel(log_level.upper())
    logger.handlers.clear()
    logger.propagate = False

    formatter = logging.Formatter(LOG_FORMAT)

    file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding="utf-8")
    file_handler.setLevel(log_level.upper())
    file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    logger.addHandler(file_handler)

    return logger
```

# 3. `src/stockdss/utilities/config.py`

Indsæt dette:

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

try:
    import yaml
except ImportError:
    yaml = None


def get_environment_variable(
    name: str,
    default: str | None = None,
    required: bool = False,
) -> str | None:
    value = os.getenv(name, default)

    if required and (value is None or value == ""):
        raise RuntimeError(f"Missing required environment variable: {name}")

    return value


def get_boolean_environment_variable(name: str, default: bool = False) -> bool:
    raw_value = os.getenv(name)

    if raw_value is None:
        return default

    return raw_value.strip().lower() in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}


def load_yaml_file(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
    if yaml is None:
        raise ImportError(
            "PyYAML is required to load YAML files. Install it with: pip install pyyaml"
        )

    if not path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"YAML file does not exist: {path}")

    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
        data = yaml.safe_load(file)

    if data is None:
        return {}

    if not isinstance(data, dict):
        raise ValueError(f"Expected YAML file to contain a dictionary: {path}")

    return data
```

# 4. `src/stockdss/utilities/seed.py`

Indsæt dette:

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import os
import random

import numpy as np


def set_global_seed(seed: int) -> None:
    """
    Set seeds for Python, NumPy and PyTorch if available.
    """
    os.environ["PYTHONHASHSEED"] = str(seed)

    random.seed(seed)
    np.random.seed(seed)

    try:
        import torch

        torch.manual_seed(seed)

        if torch.cuda.is_available():
            torch.cuda.manual_seed(seed)
            torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)

        torch.backends.cudnn.deterministic = True
        torch.backends.cudnn.benchmark = False

    except ImportError:
        pass
```

# 5. Minimal test-runner

Opret/fyld denne fil:

```text
src/stockdss/runner/run_v2_smoke_test.py
```

med:

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import sys
from pathlib import Path

from stockdss.utilities.config import get_boolean_environment_variable
from stockdss.utilities.logging import setup_run_logger, setup_system_logger
from stockdss.utilities.paths import PROJECT_ROOT, create_run_paths
from stockdss.utilities.seed import set_global_seed


def main() -> int:
    system_logger = setup_system_logger()
    system_logger.info("Starting StockDSS V2 smoke test.")
    system_logger.info("Project root: %s", PROJECT_ROOT)

    run_paths = None

    try:
        set_global_seed(42)

        use_wandb = get_boolean_environment_variable(
            "STOCKDSS_USE_WANDB",
            default=False,
        )

        run_paths = create_run_paths("v2_smoke_test")
        run_logger = setup_run_logger(run_paths)

        run_logger.info("Created run directory: %s", run_paths.run_directory)
        run_logger.info("Run id: %s", run_paths.run_id)
        run_logger.info("Weights & Biases enabled: %s", use_wandb)

        smoke_summary = {
            "status": "ok",
            "run_id": run_paths.run_id,
            "project_root": str(PROJECT_ROOT),
            "run_directory": str(run_paths.run_directory),
            "wandb_enabled": use_wandb,
            "next_step": "Add predefined strategies and FinRL data pipeline.",
        }

        summary_path = run_paths.summary_directory / "smoke_test_summary.json"

        with summary_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as file:
            json.dump(smoke_summary, file, indent=2)

        run_logger.info("Wrote smoke test summary: %s", summary_path)
        system_logger.info("StockDSS V2 smoke test completed successfully.")

        return 0

    except Exception:
        system_logger.exception("StockDSS V2 smoke test failed.")

        if run_paths is not None:
            try:
                run_logger = setup_run_logger(run_paths)
                run_logger.exception("Run failed.")
            except Exception:
                pass

        return 1


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())
```

# Vigtig regel fremadrettet

Fra nu af:

```python
run_paths = create_run_paths(...)
```

er det eneste sted, hvor run-output oprettes.

Så senere skriver vi altid sådan:

```python
decision_log_path = run_paths.audit_directory / "decision_log.csv"
model_path = run_paths.models_directory / "iqn_model.pt"
plot_path = run_paths.plots_directory / "portfolio_value.png"
summary_path = run_paths.summary_directory / "run_summary.json"
```

Ikke sådan her:

```python
"outputs/runs/..."
"results/..."
"trained_models/..."
```

Det er sådan vi undgår V1-rod.

Det betyder:

```text
Brug pathlib.Path overalt
Ingen hardcoded "\"
Ingen Windows-specifikke paths i Python-kode
Ingen afhængighed af PowerShell i selve systemet
```

Din nuværende test virker, og det er godt. Nu skal vi bare rette navngivning og gøre det mere konsekvent med **StockInvestmentDSS**.

## 1. Ja, rename fra `StockDSS` til `StockInvestmentDSS`

I dine logs står der nu:

```text
Starting StockDSS V2 smoke test.
StockDSS V2 smoke test completed successfully.
```

Det skal ændres til:

```text
Starting StockInvestmentDSS V2 smoke test.
StockInvestmentDSS V2 smoke test completed successfully.
```

Og W&B project bør også hedde:

```text
stock-investment-dss-finrl-iqn
```

eller:

```text
StockInvestmentDSS-FinRL-IQN
```

Jeg ville bruge lowercase til tooling:

```env
STOCKINVESTMENTDSS_WANDB_PROJECT=stock-investment-dss-finrl-iqn
```

Men for korthed kan vi stadig bruge env-prefix:

```env
STOCKDSS_USE_WANDB=false
```

Det er teknisk fint. Hvis du vil være helt konsekvent, bruger vi:

```env
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_USE_WANDB=false
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT=stock-investment-dss-finrl-iqn
```

Min anbefaling: **brug det lange, tydelige navn fra nu af**.

---

## 2. Opdater `.env` og `.env.example`

Brug dette:

```env
PYTHONPATH=src

STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_LOG_LEVEL=INFO

STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_USE_WANDB=false
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT=stock-investment-dss-finrl-iqn

STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DATA_SOURCE=finrl
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_CACHE_DIR=data/cache
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_OUTPUT_DIR=outputs/runs

STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_PRESET=recent_live_like_2025_2026
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_STRATEGY=balanced_growth
```

Hvis du senere slår W&B til:

```env
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_USE_WANDB=true
WANDB_API_KEY=...
```

---

## 3. Ret `utilities/config.py`

Skift ikke nødvendigvis funktionerne, men brug de nye env-navne i runneren.

Hvis du vil have en helper, kan du tilføje:

```python
def get_log_level() -> str:
    return get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_LOG_LEVEL",
        default="INFO",
    ) or "INFO"


def use_weights_and_biases() -> bool:
    return get_boolean_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_USE_WANDB",
        default=False,
    )
```

---

## 4. Ret `runner/run_smoke_test.py`

Skift teksten og env-var-navnet.

Relevant ændring:

```python
from stockdss.utilities.config import (
    get_boolean_environment_variable,
    get_environment_variable,
)
```

Og i `main()`:

```python
log_level = get_environment_variable(
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_LOG_LEVEL",
    default="INFO",
) or "INFO"

system_logger = setup_system_logger(log_level=log_level)
system_logger.info("Starting StockInvestmentDSS V2 smoke test.")
```

Og:

```python
use_wandb = get_boolean_environment_variable(
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_USE_WANDB",
    default=False,
)
```

Og til sidst:

```python
system_logger.info("StockInvestmentDSS V2 smoke test completed successfully.")
```

---

## 5. OS-uafhængighed: din Python-kode er på rette vej

Din output viser Windows paths:

```text
C:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\...
```

Det er helt fint, fordi `pathlib` renderer paths efter OS.

På Mac/Linux ville samme kode give:

```text
/Users/...
```

Det vigtige er, at vi i Python altid gør sådan:

```python
summary_path = run_paths.summary_directory / "smoke_test_summary.json"
```

Ikke sådan:

```python
summary_path = str(run_paths.summary_directory) + "\\smoke_test_summary.json"
```

Så længe vi holder den regel, virker det på Windows, macOS og Linux.

---

## 6. Du har omdøbt filen til `run_smoke_test.py` — det er fint

Din kommando:

```powershell
python -m stockdss.runner.run_smoke_test
```

er bedre end `run_v2_smoke_test.py`.

Vi beholder:

```text
src/stockdss/runner/run_smoke_test.py
```

Men selve run-name kan stadig være:

```python
run_paths = create_run_paths("v2_smoke_test")
```

Det er okay, fordi det beskriver run-typen.

Hvis du vil gøre det mere produktagtigt:

```python
run_paths = create_run_paths("smoke_test")
```

Så får du:

```text
outputs/runs/2026_05_17_040255_smoke_test/
```

Jeg ville gøre det.

---

## 7. Ret i `paths.py`: run-name skal være generisk

I runneren:

```python
run_paths = create_run_paths("smoke_test")
```

Ikke:

```python
run_paths = create_run_paths("v2_smoke_test")
```

V2 er jo selve projektfasen, men outputtet kan bare hedde smoke test.

---

## 8. Næste oprydning

Kør:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem .\src -Recurse -Directory -Filter "__pycache__" | Remove-Item -Recurse -Force
```

Og `structure.txt` kan du slette eller ignorere.

Til `.gitignore`:

```gitignore
__pycache__/
*.pyc
structure.txt

.env
.env.*
!.env.example

logs/*.log

outputs/runs/*
!outputs/runs/.gitkeep
```

---

## 9. Status

Det her er faktisk godt:

```text
system log virker
run log virker
run folder oprettes rigtigt
summary skrives rigtigt
PYTHONPATH virker
module execution virker
```

Det er præcis den slags fundament, der manglede i V1.

Næste step bør være:

```text
strategies/predefined.py
```

med de tre hardcoded strategier:

```text
defensive_preservation
balanced_growth
aggressive_growth
```

Derefter kan smoke testen udvides til at:

```text
load default strategy
copy strategy config into outputs/runs/<run_id>/config/
write strategy summary into summary/
```

Så har vi første rigtige DSS-lag på plads.

## Ryd cache og gamle test-runs

Kør:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem .\src -Recurse -Directory -Filter "__pycache__" | Remove-Item -Recurse -Force
```

Hvis du vil rydde de gamle `v2_smoke_test` runs:

```powershell
Remove-Item .\outputs\runs\*_v2_smoke_test -Recurse -Force
```

```text
2026_05_17_044514_d_iqn_dss_smoke_test
```

## Næste step

Nu er utilities-laget godkendt. Næste fil bør være:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py
```

med de tre hardcoded strategier:

```text
defensive_preservation
balanced_growth
aggressive_growth
```

Og derefter udvider vi `run_smoke_test.py`, så den loader `balanced_growth`, kopierer strategy config ind i:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/config/strategy.json
```

og skriver strategy summary i:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/summary/smoke_test_summary.json
```

ChatGPT:

Perfekt — nu er navnestandarden rettet korrekt.

Det vigtigste er, at loggerne nu bruger:

```text
stock_investment_dss.system
stock_investment_dss.run.<run_id>
```

i stedet for `stockdss.*`, og smoke testen kører korrekt med:

```powershell
python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.run_smoke_test
```

Det betyder, at **utilities-basen er godkendt**: project root findes, system logs virker, run logs virker, run directories oprettes korrekt, og summary skrives til den rigtige run-folder. 

Fejlen ved sletning:

```text
Remove-Item: The process cannot access the file ... because it is being used by another process.
```

er ikke kritisk. Det skyldes sandsynligvis, at en fil i den gamle run-folder stadig er åben i VS Code, terminal, Explorer, Dropbox-sync eller en Python/log-handler. Luk eventuelle åbne filer/foldere, vent et øjeblik på Dropbox, og prøv evt.:

```powershell
Remove-Item .\outputs\runs\*_v2_smoke_test -Recurse -Force
```

Men du behøver ikke bruge tid på det nu.

## Næste rigtige step

Nu går vi videre til første DSS-lag:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py
```

Den skal indeholde de 3 hardcoded strategier:

```text
defensive_preservation
balanced_growth
aggressive_growth
```

Og derefter udvider vi:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/runner/run_smoke_test.py
```

så den også:

```text
1. loader default strategy fra .env
2. gemmer strategy config i outputs/runs/<run_id>/config/strategy.json
3. skriver strategy-info i smoke_test_summary.json
```

Så har vi denne del på plads:

```text
Investor strategy config
↓
Run config snapshot
↓
Audit-ready output structure
```

Det er næste naturlige lag før FinRL data pipeline.

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass
from typing import Literal


RiskProfile = Literal["low", "medium", "high"]
ScoreQuantile = Literal["q25", "q50", "q75"]


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyConstraints:
    allow_shorting: bool
    allow_margin: bool
    max_position_weight: float
    max_sector_weight: float
    min_cash_weight: float
    target_cash_weight: float
    max_turnover_per_decision: float


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyRiskPolicy:
    lambda_cvar: float
    lambda_drawdown: float
    lambda_volatility: float
    lambda_transaction_cost: float
    lambda_concentration: float
    lambda_strategy_violation: float
    score_quantile: ScoreQuantile
    downside_metric: str


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyRebalanceRules:
    frequency: str
    drift_threshold: float
    force_if_position_above_max: bool


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyConfig:
    strategy_id: str
    display_name: str
    risk_profile: RiskProfile
    objective: str
    description: str
    constraints: StrategyConstraints
    risk_policy: StrategyRiskPolicy
    allowed_actions: tuple[str, ...]
    rebalance: StrategyRebalanceRules
    evaluation_metrics: tuple[str, ...]

    def to_dict(self) -> dict:
        return asdict(self)
