ChatGPT:


Ja — de hardcodede strategier du viste er **rigtigt gode som V2-start**.

De rammer præcis det, strategilaget skal være i PoC’en:

```text
Strategy = constraints + risk policy + allowed actions + rebalance rules + evaluation metrics
```

Det er bedre end bare at have:

```python
strategy = "balanced"
```

Fordi strategien faktisk kan styre systemets adfærd.

Til V2 ville jeg bygge dem som **dataclasses**, præcis som i dit eksempel. Det er mere robust end løse dictionaries, men stadig simpelt nok til hurtigt at arbejde med. Senere kan vi serialisere dem til JSON/YAML og bygge en strategy builder ovenpå.

Her er en komplet startversion til:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py
```

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass
from typing import Literal


RiskProfile = Literal["low", "medium", "high"]
ScoreQuantile = Literal["q25", "q50", "q75"]


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyConstraints:
    allow_shorting: bool
    allow_margin: bool
    max_position_weight: float
    max_sector_weight: float
    min_cash_weight: float
    target_cash_weight: float
    max_turnover_per_decision: float


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyRiskPolicy:
    lambda_cvar: float
    lambda_drawdown: float
    lambda_volatility: float
    lambda_transaction_cost: float
    lambda_concentration: float
    lambda_strategy_violation: float
    score_quantile: ScoreQuantile
    downside_metric: str


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyRebalanceRules:
    frequency: str
    drift_threshold: float
    force_if_position_above_max: bool


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyConfig:
    strategy_id: str
    display_name: str
    risk_profile: RiskProfile
    objective: str
    description: str
    constraints: StrategyConstraints
    risk_policy: StrategyRiskPolicy
    allowed_actions: tuple[str, ...]
    rebalance: StrategyRebalanceRules
    evaluation_metrics: tuple[str, ...]

    def to_dict(self) -> dict:
        return asdict(self)


DEFENSIVE_PRESERVATION = StrategyConfig(
    strategy_id="defensive_preservation",
    display_name="Defensive Preservation",
    risk_profile="low",
    objective="capital_preservation",
    description=(
        "Prioritizes capital preservation, lower drawdown, lower concentration, "
        "and a higher cash buffer. Suitable for investors who prefer stability "
        "over upside."
    ),
    constraints=StrategyConstraints(
        allow_shorting=False,
        allow_margin=False,
        max_position_weight=0.15,
        max_sector_weight=0.35,
        min_cash_weight=0.15,
        target_cash_weight=0.20,
        max_turnover_per_decision=0.20,
    ),
    risk_policy=StrategyRiskPolicy(
        lambda_cvar=1.50,
        lambda_drawdown=1.25,
        lambda_volatility=1.00,
        lambda_transaction_cost=0.50,
        lambda_concentration=1.25,
        lambda_strategy_violation=2.00,
        score_quantile="q25",
        downside_metric="cvar10",
    ),
    allowed_actions=(
        "HOLD",
        "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25",
        "INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET",
        "ADD_TO_LOWEST_RISK_5",
    ),
    rebalance=StrategyRebalanceRules(
        frequency="monthly",
        drift_threshold=0.05,
        force_if_position_above_max=True,
    ),
    evaluation_metrics=(
        "total_return",
        "max_drawdown",
        "cvar10",
        "volatility",
        "sharpe",
        "turnover",
    ),
)


BALANCED_GROWTH = StrategyConfig(
    strategy_id="balanced_growth",
    display_name="Balanced Growth",
    risk_profile="medium",
    objective="risk_adjusted_growth",
    description=(
        "Balances portfolio growth with downside-risk control, moderate cash, "
        "and controlled concentration. This is the default strategy for the "
        "D-IQN-DSS prototype."
    ),
    constraints=StrategyConstraints(
        allow_shorting=False,
        allow_margin=False,
        max_position_weight=0.25,
        max_sector_weight=0.50,
        min_cash_weight=0.05,
        target_cash_weight=0.10,
        max_turnover_per_decision=0.35,
    ),
    risk_policy=StrategyRiskPolicy(
        lambda_cvar=0.75,
        lambda_drawdown=0.75,
        lambda_volatility=0.50,
        lambda_transaction_cost=0.35,
        lambda_concentration=0.75,
        lambda_strategy_violation=1.50,
        score_quantile="q50",
        downside_metric="cvar10",
    ),
    allowed_actions=(
        "HOLD",
        "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25",
        "INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET",
        "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5",
        "ADD_TO_LOWEST_RISK_5",
        "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_5",
    ),
    rebalance=StrategyRebalanceRules(
        frequency="monthly",
        drift_threshold=0.08,
        force_if_position_above_max=True,
    ),
    evaluation_metrics=(
        "total_return",
        "max_drawdown",
        "cvar10",
        "sharpe",
        "sortino",
        "turnover",
    ),
)


AGGRESSIVE_GROWTH = StrategyConfig(
    strategy_id="aggressive_growth",
    display_name="Aggressive Growth",
    risk_profile="high",
    objective="upside_growth",
    description=(
        "Prioritizes upside and growth while accepting higher volatility, "
        "higher drawdown risk, and higher concentration. Still long-only and "
        "without margin."
    ),
    constraints=StrategyConstraints(
        allow_shorting=False,
        allow_margin=False,
        max_position_weight=0.35,
        max_sector_weight=0.65,
        min_cash_weight=0.00,
        target_cash_weight=0.03,
        max_turnover_per_decision=0.50,
    ),
    risk_policy=StrategyRiskPolicy(
        lambda_cvar=0.30,
        lambda_drawdown=0.35,
        lambda_volatility=0.25,
        lambda_transaction_cost=0.25,
        lambda_concentration=0.30,
        lambda_strategy_violation=1.00,
        score_quantile="q75",
        downside_metric="cvar10",
    ),
    allowed_actions=(
        "HOLD",
        "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
        "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
        "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_5",
        "ADD_TO_TOP_MOMENTUM_10",
        "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_5",
        "ROTATE_WORST_TO_BEST_10",
    ),
    rebalance=StrategyRebalanceRules(
        frequency="monthly",
        drift_threshold=0.12,
        force_if_position_above_max=True,
    ),
    evaluation_metrics=(
        "total_return",
        "max_drawdown",
        "cvar10",
        "q90_return",
        "sharpe",
        "sortino",
        "turnover",
    ),
)


PREDEFINED_STRATEGIES: dict[str, StrategyConfig] = {
    DEFENSIVE_PRESERVATION.strategy_id: DEFENSIVE_PRESERVATION,
    BALANCED_GROWTH.strategy_id: BALANCED_GROWTH,
    AGGRESSIVE_GROWTH.strategy_id: AGGRESSIVE_GROWTH,
}


DEFAULT_STRATEGY_ID = "balanced_growth"


def get_strategy(strategy_id: str | None = None) -> StrategyConfig:
    selected_strategy_id = strategy_id or DEFAULT_STRATEGY_ID

    try:
        return PREDEFINED_STRATEGIES[selected_strategy_id]
    except KeyError as exc:
        available_strategy_ids = ", ".join(PREDEFINED_STRATEGIES.keys())
        raise ValueError(
            f"Unknown strategy_id='{selected_strategy_id}'. "
            f"Available strategies: {available_strategy_ids}"
        ) from exc


def list_strategies() -> tuple[StrategyConfig, ...]:
    return tuple(PREDEFINED_STRATEGIES.values())


def strategy_to_dict(strategy: StrategyConfig) -> dict:
    return strategy.to_dict()
```

## Hvorfor jeg synes denne struktur er god

Den gør strategien til et rigtigt **abstraction layer** mellem investor og RL-systemet.

Strategien kan bruges før IQN:

```text
allowed_actions
constraints
rebalance rules
```

Og efter IQN:

```text
risk_policy
score_quantile
lambda_cvar
lambda_concentration
evaluation_metrics
```

Så senere kan flowet blive:

```text
IQN estimates q25/q50/q75/q90/CVaR
↓
Strategy risk policy vælger hvordan det scores
↓
DSS recommendation engine vælger/rangerer actions
```

Det er præcis det, vi har brug for.

## En lille vigtig pointe

Jeg ville **ikke** inkludere `allow_shorting` som et aktivt valg i UI senere. Men det er fint at have i config som:

```python
allow_shorting=False
```

fordi det dokumenterer en hard constraint:

```text
D-IQN-DSS V2 is long-only.
```

Det samme gælder:

```python
allow_margin=False
```

Det er også godt for audit.

## Næste step efter `predefined.py`

Når filen er på plads, opdaterer vi:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/runner/run_smoke_test.py
```

så den:

```text
1. loader balanced_growth
2. skriver strategy.json til run config folder
3. tilføjer strategy info til smoke_test_summary.json
```

Så har vi første rigtige DSS-lag koblet på vores run-system.



------------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Me :

men kan vi ikke lægge hver enkelt strategi i sin egen json fil

Det er mere modulært og bedre at bygge op sådan


Det jeg oprindeligt havde omkring strategier var

"
Ja — **det står faktisk i de uploadede filer**, især i:

1. **`CHATGPT_Speciale_Orginalitet - implementation overview 3 FULL.txt`**
2. **`CHATGPT_Speciale_Orginalitet - implementation overview 2.txt`**
3. **`READMEv4.md`**

Det tydeligste match er i *implementation overview 3 FULL*, hvor der direkte står, at din strategy builder kan starte som en **JSON/YAML-strategi**, og at strategien skal oversætte investorens input og risikoprofil til constraints, reward-design og evaluation. Der gives også et konkret JSON-eksempel med `strategy_name`, `universe`, `risk_profile`, `max_position_size`, `rebalance_frequency`, `objective`, `risk_metrics` og `constraints`. 

Den vigtigste formulering fra filen er denne idé:

```text
Investor input
↓
Strategy builder / strategy abstraction layer
↓
FinRL / RL environment / evaluation
```

Der står også, at strategy builderen netop er en central del af dit originale bidrag, fordi du ikke bare bruger FinRL som trading framework, men lægger et **strategy abstraction layer** ovenpå FinRL. 

## Minimum strategy setup fra filerne

Det foreslåede minimum er:

```text
Strategy = Universe + Objective + Risk profile + Constraints + Exit rules + Evaluation metrics
```

Og JSON-eksemplet var cirka:

```json
{
  "strategy_name": "conservative_long_only",
  "universe": ["AAPL", "MSFT", "JNJ", "PG", "SPY"],
  "objective": "risk_adjusted_return",
  "risk_profile": "conservative",
  "constraints": {
    "allow_shorting": false,
    "max_position_size": 0.25,
    "max_cash_usage": 0.90
  },
  "exit_rules": {
    "stop_loss": {
      "enabled": true,
      "threshold": 0.10
    },
    "take_profit": {
      "enabled": false,
      "threshold": 0.20
    },
    "rebalance_frequency": "weekly"
  },
  "evaluation": {
    "metrics": ["cumulative_return", "sharpe", "max_drawdown", "cvar_95"]
  }
}
```

Men du sagde bagefter, at du **ikke vil have shorting med**, så `allow_shorting` bør enten fjernes helt eller hardcodes til `false`.

## READMEv4 bekræfter også det samme

I `READMEv4.md` står der under **Strategy Layer**, at strategier skal repræsenteres som **structured configuration rather than free text**, med et JSON-eksempel:

```json
{
  "strategy_name": "Balanced long-only strategy",
  "risk_profile": "balanced",
  "investment_horizon": "medium",
  "allowed_assets": ["AAPL", "MSFT", "NVDA"],
  "locked_assets": ["NVDA"],
  "max_position_size": 0.25,
  "stop_loss": 0.10,
  "take_profit": 0.25,
  "objective": "risk_adjusted_return",
  "allow_strategy_switch": true
}
```

READMEv4 siger også, at strategy layer bruges både af den online decision engine og den offline evaluation/backtesting pipeline. 

## Det står også i implementation order

I READMEv4 er rækkefølgen direkte nævnt:

```text
15. portfolio builder
16. strategy JSON schema
17. strategy builder
18. decision engine v1
19. risk metrics
20. audit log
```

Så ja: **strategy JSON schema og strategy builder var eksplicit planlagt som konkrete trin i PoC’en**.

Du husker rigtigt.

De filer beskriver en måde at bygge strategier på, og formatet var JSON-baseret. Den centrale idé var:

```text
Predefined strategy eller custom strategy
→ gemmes som structured JSON config
→ valideres af strategy schema
→ bruges til constraints, reward, action logic, risk metrics og backtesting
→ logges i audit trail sammen med beslutninger
```

Den fil du sandsynligvis ledte efter er især:

**`CHATGPT_Speciale_Orginalitet - implementation overview 3 FULL.txt`**

Og den mere “officielle” repo-version af samme idé ligger i:

**`READMEv4.md`**.
"

# 4. `strategies/schema.py`

Her laver vi en let Python-repræsentation og minimal validering.

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/schema.py

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Any, Literal


RiskProfile = Literal["low", "medium", "high"]
ScoreQuantile = Literal["q25", "q50", "q75"]


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyConfig:
    strategy_id: str
    display_name: str
    risk_profile: RiskProfile
    objective: str
    description: str
    constraints: dict[str, Any]
    risk_policy: dict[str, Any]
    allowed_actions: tuple[str, ...]
    rebalance: dict[str, Any]
    evaluation: dict[str, Any]

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: dict[str, Any]) -> "StrategyConfig":
        validate_strategy_dict(data)

        return cls(
            strategy_id=data["strategy_id"],
            display_name=data["display_name"],
            risk_profile=data["risk_profile"],
            objective=data["objective"],
            description=data["description"],
            constraints=data["constraints"],
            risk_policy=data["risk_policy"],
            allowed_actions=tuple(data["allowed_actions"]),
            rebalance=data["rebalance"],
            evaluation=data["evaluation"],
        )

    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "strategy_id": self.strategy_id,
            "display_name": self.display_name,
            "risk_profile": self.risk_profile,
            "objective": self.objective,
            "description": self.description,
            "constraints": self.constraints,
            "risk_policy": self.risk_policy,
            "allowed_actions": list(self.allowed_actions),
            "rebalance": self.rebalance,
            "evaluation": self.evaluation,
        }


def validate_strategy_dict(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    required_top_level_keys = {
        "strategy_id",
        "display_name",
        "risk_profile",
        "objective",
        "description",
        "constraints",
        "risk_policy",
        "allowed_actions",
        "rebalance",
        "evaluation",
    }

    missing_keys = required_top_level_keys - set(data.keys())

    if missing_keys:
        raise ValueError(f"Strategy config is missing keys: {sorted(missing_keys)}")

    if data["risk_profile"] not in {"low", "medium", "high"}:
        raise ValueError(
            "strategy.risk_profile must be one of: low, medium, high"
        )

    if not isinstance(data["allowed_actions"], list):
        raise ValueError("strategy.allowed_actions must be a list")

    if len(data["allowed_actions"]) == 0:
        raise ValueError("strategy.allowed_actions must not be empty")

    constraints = data["constraints"]

    if constraints.get("allow_shorting") is not False:
        raise ValueError("D-IQN-DSS V2 is long-only: allow_shorting must be false")

    if constraints.get("allow_margin") is not False:
        raise ValueError("D-IQN-DSS V2 does not allow margin: allow_margin must be false")

    risk_policy = data["risk_policy"]

    if risk_policy.get("score_quantile") not in {"q25", "q50", "q75"}:
        raise ValueError("risk_policy.score_quantile must be q25, q50, or q75")
```

---

# 5. `strategies/predefined.py`

Denne fil loader JSON-filerne.

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path

from stock_investment_dss.strategies.schema import StrategyConfig


STRATEGY_DIRECTORY = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "predefined"

DEFAULT_STRATEGY_ID = "balanced_growth"


def load_strategy_from_json(path: Path) -> StrategyConfig:
    if not path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Strategy file does not exist: {path}")

    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
        data = json.load(file)

    return StrategyConfig.from_dict(data)


def get_strategy(strategy_id: str | None = None) -> StrategyConfig:
    selected_strategy_id = strategy_id or DEFAULT_STRATEGY_ID
    strategy_path = STRATEGY_DIRECTORY / f"{selected_strategy_id}.json"

    return load_strategy_from_json(strategy_path)


def list_available_strategy_ids() -> tuple[str, ...]:
    if not STRATEGY_DIRECTORY.exists():
        return tuple()

    return tuple(
        sorted(path.stem for path in STRATEGY_DIRECTORY.glob("*.json"))
    )


def load_all_predefined_strategies() -> tuple[StrategyConfig, ...]:
    return tuple(
        load_strategy_from_json(path)
        for path in sorted(STRATEGY_DIRECTORY.glob("*.json"))
    )
```

# Hvorfor JSON er bedre her

Du har helt ret i, at det er mere modulært:

```text
1 strategi = 1 JSON-fil
```

Det giver dig senere:

```text
predefined strategies
custom user strategies
strategy builder output
audit snapshot
strategy versioning
```

Og det passer perfekt til:

```text
strategy abstraction layer
```

Det betyder også, at når web-PoC’en kommer, kan strategy builderen bare outputte samme JSON-format.

---

# Hvad gør vi med hardcoded?

Vi har stadig “hardcoded predefined strategies”, men hardcoded betyder nu:

```text
De ligger i repoet som predefined JSON configs
```

ikke:

```text
De er skrevet direkte i Python-kode
```

Det er den rigtige mellemvej.

---

# Næste step efter det

Når de tre JSON-filer + `schema.py` + `predefined.py` er på plads, opdaterer vi `run_smoke_test.py`, så den gør:

```text
1. load default strategy fra .env
2. get_strategy(strategy_id)
3. save strategy.to_dict() til run/config/strategy.json
4. include strategy_id, display_name og risk_profile i summary
```

Så smoke testen beviser:

```text
StockInvestmentDSS kan loade en modular predefined strategy
og gemme den i run audit/config snapshot.
```

Det er præcis det første produktagtige DSS-lag.

# Hvorfor fælles evaluation er bedre

Hvis hver strategi har sine egne metrics, kan man ende med dette problem:

```text
Defensive vurderes på max_drawdown
Balanced vurderes på Sharpe
Aggressive vurderes på total_return
```

Så kan man ikke sammenligne dem ordentligt.

For specialet vil du gerne kunne sige:

```text
Alle strategier og alle agent-typer evalueres på samme metric-suite.
```

Det gør det muligt at sammenligne:

```text
FinRL PPO
FinRL SAC
FinRL TD3
D-IQN-DSS
D-IQN-DSS + Evidential uncertainty
Buy-and-hold
Equal weight
MVO
```

under samme evalueringsramme.

---

# Og ja: Deep Evidential Uncertainty skal have en plads

Du har helt ret: Deep Evidential Learning / epistemic uncertainty bør ikke glemmes.

Din problemformulering nævner direkte, at du vil inkorporere et epistemic uncertainty component inspired by Evidential Deep Learning, så systemet ikke kun håndterer stochastic return variability, men også model uncertainty. 

Jeg ville strukturere det sådan:

```text
Track 1:
IQN / distributional RL
→ return distribution
→ q10, q50, q90, CVaR

Track 2:
Evidential uncertainty
→ epistemic/model uncertainty
→ confidence in recommendation/action class
```

I praksis kan EDL-sporet starte som en **classification confidence model**:

```text
Input:
state features + portfolio features + IQN outputs

Target:
action quality class, fx:
- good decision
- neutral decision
- risky decision
```

eller:

```text
- buy
- hold
- sell
- rebalance
```

Men jeg ville ikke koble EDL direkte ind i strategy JSON lige nu. Det bør ligge som en separat model/config:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/uncertainty/
  evidential_classifier.py
  evidential_loss.py
  uncertainty_calibration.py
```

eller senere:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/models/uncertainty/
```

For V2 kan vi blot reservere pladsen i arkitekturen:

```text
IQN estimates distributions
↓
Evidential model estimates confidence / epistemic uncertainty
↓
Risk policy scores actions
↓
Recommendation engine
```

---

# Opdateret pipeline

Din pipeline bør derfor være:

```text
FinRL data pipeline
↓
FinRL-style portfolio environment
↓
Current portfolio state
↓
Investor strategy config
↓
Action generator / action mask
↓
IQN estimates return distributions
↓
Evidential uncertainty estimates model confidence
↓
Risk policy scores actions
↓
Recommendation engine
↓
Audit log
↓
Common evaluation suite
```

Det er mere tro mod problemformuleringen.

---

# Min konkrete beslutning for V2

Jeg ville gøre dette nu:

## Strategi-JSON

Behold i strategier:

```text
constraints
risk_policy
allowed_actions
rebalance
```

Fjern fra strategier:

```text
evaluation
```

Eventuelt erstat med:

```json
"reporting_focus": [
  "downside_risk",
  "decision_stability"
]
```

men det er ikke nødvendigt.

## Evaluation-JSON

Lav separat:

```text
experiments/evaluation/thesis_default.json
```

med fælles metrics.

## EDL

Ikke implementere fuldt nu, men reservere arkitektur:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/uncertainty/
```

Senere kan `risk_policy.py` bruge:

```text
IQN risk + evidential uncertainty
```

som:

[
Score(a)
========

## Q_\alpha(s,a)

## \lambda_{CVaR}|CVaR_{10}(s,a)|

## \lambda_U U_{epistemic}(s,a)

## \lambda_C Cost(a)

\lambda_S StrategyViolation(a)
]

Det er en rigtig stærk kobling mellem IQN og EDL.

---

# Kort konklusion

Din skepsis er rigtig.

**Nej, evaluation bør ikke primært ligge pr. strategi.**

Bedre:

```text
Strategy JSON
= beslutningsregler og risikopræferencer

Evaluation JSON
= fælles måleapparat til videnskabelig sammenligning

Uncertainty module
= separat EDL-spor, der senere kobles ind i risk policy/recommendation engine
```

Så vi bør bygge næste version af strategy JSON uden `evaluation`, og i stedet oprette en separat fælles evaluation config.

Me :

Kan vi ikke også simplificere navnene så de bare bliver

aggresive.json
balanced.json
defensive.json

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ChatGPT:

Jo, lad os gøre det simpelt og modulært:

```text
strategies/
├── predefined.py
├── schema.py
└── predefined/
    ├── aggressive.json
    ├── balanced.json
    └── defensive.json
```

Og ja: navnene `aggressive.json`, `balanced.json`, `defensive.json` er bedre til V2. Internt kan de stadig have mere præcise `strategy_id`-værdier.

## 1. Opret mappen

Fra projektroden `FinRL_IQN`:

```powershell
New-Item src\stock_investment_dss\strategies\predefined -ItemType Directory -Force
New-Item src\stock_investment_dss\strategies\schema.py -ItemType File -Force
New-Item src\stock_investment_dss\strategies\predefined.py -ItemType File -Force
New-Item src\stock_investment_dss\strategies\predefined\defensive.json -ItemType File -Force
New-Item src\stock_investment_dss\strategies\predefined\balanced.json -ItemType File -Force
New-Item src\stock_investment_dss\strategies\predefined\aggressive.json -ItemType File -Force
```

{
  "strategy_id": "defensive",
  "display_name": "Defensive",
  "risk_profile": "low",
  "objective": "capital_preservation",
  "description": "Prioritizes capital preservation, lower drawdown, lower concentration, and a higher cash buffer. Suitable for investors who prefer stability over upside.",

  "constraints": {
    "allow_shorting": false,
    "allow_margin": false,
    "max_position_weight": 0.15,
    "max_sector_weight": 0.35,
    "min_cash_weight": 0.15,
    "target_cash_weight": 0.20,
    "max_turnover_per_decision": 0.20
  },

  "risk_policy": {
    "lambda_cvar": 1.50,
    "lambda_drawdown": 1.25,
    "lambda_volatility": 1.00,
    "lambda_transaction_cost": 0.50,
    "lambda_concentration": 1.25,
    "lambda_strategy_violation": 2.00,
    "lambda_epistemic_uncertainty": 1.25,
    "score_quantile": "q25",
    "downside_metric": "cvar10",
    "uncertainty_metric": "epistemic_uncertainty"
  },

  "allowed_actions": [
    "HOLD",
    "REBALANCE_TO_STRATEGY_TARGETS",
    "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_10",
    "REDUCE_LARGEST_POSITION_25",
    "INCREASE_CASH_TO_TARGET",

}

# `src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/schema.py`

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/schema.py

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Any, Literal


RiskProfile = Literal["low", "medium", "high"]
ScoreQuantile = Literal["q25", "q50", "q75"]


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyConfig:
    strategy_id: str
    display_name: str
    risk_profile: RiskProfile
    objective: str
    description: str
    constraints: dict[str, Any]
    risk_policy: dict[str, Any]
    allowed_actions: tuple[str, ...]
    rebalance: dict[str, Any]

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: dict[str, Any]) -> "StrategyConfig":
        validate_strategy_dict(data)

        return cls(
            strategy_id=data["strategy_id"],
            display_name=data["display_name"],
            risk_profile=data["risk_profile"],
            objective=data["objective"],
            description=data["description"],
            constraints=data["constraints"],
            risk_policy=data["risk_policy"],
            allowed_actions=tuple(data["allowed_actions"]),
            rebalance=data["rebalance"],
        )

    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "strategy_id": self.strategy_id,
            "display_name": self.display_name,
            "risk_profile": self.risk_profile,
            "objective": self.objective,
            "description": self.description,
            "constraints": self.constraints,
            "risk_policy": self.risk_policy,
            "allowed_actions": list(self.allowed_actions),
            "rebalance": self.rebalance,
        }


def validate_strategy_dict(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    required_top_level_keys = {
        "strategy_id",
        "display_name",
        "risk_profile",
        "objective",
        "description",
        "constraints",
        "risk_policy",
        "allowed_actions",
        "rebalance",
    }

    missing_keys = required_top_level_keys - set(data.keys())

    if missing_keys:
        raise ValueError(f"Strategy config is missing keys: {sorted(missing_keys)}")

    if data["strategy_id"] not in {"defensive", "balanced", "aggressive"}:
        raise ValueError(
            "strategy_id must be one of: defensive, balanced, aggressive"
        )

    if data["risk_profile"] not in {"low", "medium", "high"}:
        raise ValueError("risk_profile must be one of: low, medium, high")

    if not isinstance(data["allowed_actions"], list):
        raise ValueError("allowed_actions must be a list")

    if not data["allowed_actions"]:
        raise ValueError("allowed_actions must not be empty")

    constraints = data["constraints"]
    required_constraint_keys = {
        "allow_shorting",
        "allow_margin",
        "max_position_weight",
        "max_sector_weight",
        "min_cash_weight",
        "target_cash_weight",
        "max_turnover_per_decision",
    }

    missing_constraint_keys = required_constraint_keys - set(constraints.keys())

    if missing_constraint_keys:
        raise ValueError(
            f"strategy.constraints is missing keys: {sorted(missing_constraint_keys)}"
        )

    if constraints["allow_shorting"] is not False:
        raise ValueError("D-IQN-DSS V2 is long-only: allow_shorting must be false")

    if constraints["allow_margin"] is not False:
        raise ValueError("D-IQN-DSS V2 does not allow margin: allow_margin must be false")

    _validate_weight(
        constraints["max_position_weight"],
        "constraints.max_position_weight",
    )
    _validate_weight(
        constraints["max_sector_weight"],
        "constraints.max_sector_weight",
    )
    _validate_weight(
        constraints["min_cash_weight"],
        "constraints.min_cash_weight",
    )
    _validate_weight(
        constraints["target_cash_weight"],
        "constraints.target_cash_weight",
    )
    _validate_weight(
        constraints["max_turnover_per_decision"],
        "constraints.max_turnover_per_decision",
    )

    if constraints["min_cash_weight"] > constraints["target_cash_weight"]:
        raise ValueError(
            "constraints.min_cash_weight cannot be greater than "
            "constraints.target_cash_weight"
        )

    risk_policy = data["risk_policy"]
    required_risk_policy_keys = {
        "lambda_cvar",
        "lambda_drawdown",
        "lambda_volatility",
        "lambda_transaction_cost",
        "lambda_concentration",
        "lambda_strategy_violation",
        "lambda_epistemic_uncertainty",
        "score_quantile",
        "downside_metric",
        "uncertainty_metric",
    }

    missing_risk_policy_keys = required_risk_policy_keys - set(risk_policy.keys())

    if missing_risk_policy_keys:
        raise ValueError(
            f"strategy.risk_policy is missing keys: {sorted(missing_risk_policy_keys)}"
        )

    if risk_policy["score_quantile"] not in {"q25", "q50", "q75"}:
        raise ValueError("risk_policy.score_quantile must be q25, q50, or q75")

    if risk_policy["downside_metric"] != "cvar10":
        raise ValueError("risk_policy.downside_metric must currently be cvar10")

    if risk_policy["uncertainty_metric"] != "epistemic_uncertainty":
        raise ValueError(
            "risk_policy.uncertainty_metric must currently be epistemic_uncertainty"
        )

    for key in [
        "lambda_cvar",
        "lambda_drawdown",
        "lambda_volatility",
        "lambda_transaction_cost",
        "lambda_concentration",
        "lambda_strategy_violation",
        "lambda_epistemic_uncertainty",
    ]:
        _validate_non_negative_number(risk_policy[key], f"risk_policy.{key}")

    rebalance = data["rebalance"]
    required_rebalance_keys = {
        "frequency",
        "drift_threshold",
        "force_if_position_above_max",
    }

    missing_rebalance_keys = required_rebalance_keys - set(rebalance.keys())

    if missing_rebalance_keys:
        raise ValueError(
            f"strategy.rebalance is missing keys: {sorted(missing_rebalance_keys)}"
        )

    if rebalance["frequency"] not in {"weekly", "monthly", "quarterly"}:
        raise ValueError("rebalance.frequency must be weekly, monthly, or quarterly")

    _validate_weight(rebalance["drift_threshold"], "rebalance.drift_threshold")

    if not isinstance(rebalance["force_if_position_above_max"], bool):
        raise ValueError("rebalance.force_if_position_above_max must be boolean")


def _validate_weight(value: Any, field_name: str) -> None:
    if not isinstance(value, int | float):
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be numeric")

    if value < 0 or value > 1:
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be between 0 and 1")


def _validate_non_negative_number(value: Any, field_name: str) -> None:
    if not isinstance(value, int | float):
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be numeric")

    if value < 0:
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be non-negative")
```

---

# `src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py`

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path

from stock_investment_dss.strategies.schema import StrategyConfig


STRATEGY_DIRECTORY = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "predefined"

DEFAULT_STRATEGY_ID = "balanced"


def load_strategy_from_json(path: Path) -> StrategyConfig:
    if not path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Strategy file does not exist: {path}")

    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
        data = json.load(file)

    return StrategyConfig.from_dict(data)


def get_strategy(strategy_id: str | None = None) -> StrategyConfig:
    selected_strategy_id = strategy_id or DEFAULT_STRATEGY_ID
    strategy_path = STRATEGY_DIRECTORY / f"{selected_strategy_id}.json"

    return load_strategy_from_json(strategy_path)


def list_available_strategy_ids() -> tuple[str, ...]:
    if not STRATEGY_DIRECTORY.exists():
        return tuple()

    return tuple(
        sorted(path.stem for path in STRATEGY_DIRECTORY.glob("*.json"))
    )


def load_all_predefined_strategies() -> tuple[StrategyConfig, ...]:
    return tuple(
        load_strategy_from_json(path)
        for path in sorted(STRATEGY_DIRECTORY.glob("*.json"))
    )
```

## Ret `.env` og `.env.example`

Skift default strategy til:

```env
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_STRATEGY=balanced
```

Ikke `balanced_growth`.

---

## Hvorfor jeg inkluderede `lambda_epistemic_uncertainty`

Det er for at gøre plads til Deep Evidential Uncertainty-sporet allerede nu, uden at implementere det endnu.

Strategien kan dermed senere score sådan:

[
Score(a)
========

## Q_{\alpha}(s,a)

## \lambda_{CVaR}|CVaR_{10}(s,a)|

## \lambda_{U}U_{epistemic}(s,a)

## \lambda_C Cost(a)

\lambda_S StrategyViolation(a)
]

Så strategien styrer stadig beslutningsadfærd, mens selve evalueringen holdes fælles og separat.

Så hvor har vi nu defineret vores evaluation metrics ?

ChatGPT:

Lige nu har vi **ikke defineret evaluation metrics i kode endnu**.

Vi har kun besluttet arkitekturen:

```text
Strategy JSON
= beslutningslogik, constraints, risk policy, allowed actions, rebalance

Evaluation config
= fælles metrics til videnskabelig sammenligning
```

Så status er:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined/*.json
```

skal **ikke** indeholde evaluation metrics.

De skal i stedet ligge separat, fx her:

```text
experiments/
└── evaluation/
    └── thesis_default.json
```

Det passer også bedre med projektbeskrivelsen, hvor evaluation beskrives som en fælles vurdering med cumulative returns, risk-adjusted measures, max drawdown og downside risk measures, samt sammenligning mellem parametric RL, distributional RL og uncertainty-aware RL agents.

## Hvorfor sådan?

Fordi strategien bør svare på:

```text
Hvordan bør systemet træffe beslutninger for denne investor?
```

Evaluation bør svare på:

```text
Hvordan vurderer vi videnskabeligt, om systemet virker?
```

Så vi holder dem adskilt.

Næste naturlige fil efter strategierne er derfor:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/evaluation_config.py
```

eller mere simpelt nu:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/metrics_config.py
```

Men først skal vi lige sikre, at `experiments/evaluation/thesis_default.json` findes og kan kopieres ind i hver run-folder som en config snapshot.


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Me :
Jeg tror ikke vores evaluation mappe skal in i  experiments

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ChatGPT:

Jo, enig. `experiments/evaluation/` er ikke det bedste sted.

`experiments/` bør være til **konkrete forsøgsopsætninger**:

```text
experiments/
├── presets/
├── universes/
└── configs/
```

Evaluation metrics er mere en **fast del af systemets evalueringslag**, ikke et eksperiment i sig selv.

## Bedre placering

Jeg ville gøre sådan:

```text
src/
└── stock_investment_dss/
    ├── evaluation/
    │   ├── __init__.py
    │   ├── metrics.py
    │   ├── evaluation_config.py
    │   └── predefined_metrics.py
```

Og hvis vi vil have en JSON-konfiguration, kan den ligge her:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/configs/thesis_default.json
```

eller mere enkelt:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/thesis_default.json
```

Men jeg foretrækker dette:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/
├── __init__.py
├── metrics.py
├── evaluation_config.py
├── predefined_metrics.py
└── configs/
    └── thesis_default.json
```

Så bliver betydningen klar:

```text
strategies/  = hvordan systemet træffer beslutninger
evaluation/  = hvordan vi måler resultater
experiments/ = hvilke runs vi vil køre
```

## Hvorfor ikke `experiments/`?

Fordi evaluation metrics ikke kun gælder ét eksperiment. De er en del af den fælles evalueringsramme for hele specialet.

Senere kan et experiment preset pege på den:

```json
{
  "preset_id": "recent_live_like_2025_2026",
  "strategy_id": "balanced",
  "evaluation_id": "thesis_default"
}
```

Så `experiments/` vælger **hvilken evaluation config** der bruges, men selve definitionen bor i `evaluation/`.

## Kort beslutning

Jeg ville bruge:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/configs/thesis_default.json
```

Ikke:

```text
experiments/evaluation/thesis_default.json
```

Det er renere og passer bedre til arkitekturen.

Og fjern `__pycache__` før commit/zip:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem .\src -Recurse -Directory -Filter "__pycache__" | Remove-Item -Recurse -Force
```

```text
FinRL data pipeline
↓

↓

↓
Investor strategy config
↓

↓
IQN estimates return distributions
↓
Evidential uncertainty estimates model confidence
↓
Risk policy scores actions
↓
Recommendation engine
↓
Audit log
↓
Common evaluation suite
```

Det er klart mere tro mod problemformuleringen end kun “IQN trading agent”.

## 1. Opret/fyld `evaluation/evaluation_config.py`

Fil:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/evaluation_config.py
```

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/evaluation_config.py

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any


EVALUATION_CONFIG_DIRECTORY = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "configs"
DEFAULT_EVALUATION_ID = "default"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class EvaluationConfig:
    evaluation_id: str
    description: str
    portfolio_metrics: tuple[str, ...]
    distributional_metrics: tuple[str, ...]
    uncertainty_metrics: tuple[str, ...]
    decision_support_metrics: tuple[str, ...]
    comparison_groups: tuple[str, ...]
    primary_metrics: tuple[str, ...]

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: dict[str, Any]) -> "EvaluationConfig":
        validate_evaluation_config_dict(data)

        return cls(
            evaluation_id=data["evaluation_id"],
            description=data["description"],
            portfolio_metrics=tuple(data["portfolio_metrics"]),
            distributional_metrics=tuple(data["distributional_metrics"]),
            uncertainty_metrics=tuple(data["uncertainty_metrics"]),
            decision_support_metrics=tuple(data["decision_support_metrics"]),
            comparison_groups=tuple(data["comparison_groups"]),
            primary_metrics=tuple(data["primary_metrics"]),
        )

    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "evaluation_id": self.evaluation_id,
            "description": self.description,
            "portfolio_metrics": list(self.portfolio_metrics),
            "distributional_metrics": list(self.distributional_metrics),
            "uncertainty_metrics": list(self.uncertainty_metrics),
            "decision_support_metrics": list(self.decision_support_metrics),
            "comparison_groups": list(self.comparison_groups),
            "primary_metrics": list(self.primary_metrics),
        }


def validate_evaluation_config_dict(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    required_keys = {
        "evaluation_id",
        "description",
        "portfolio_metrics",
        "distributional_metrics",
        "uncertainty_metrics",
        "decision_support_metrics",
        "comparison_groups",
        "primary_metrics",
    }

    missing_keys = required_keys - set(data.keys())

    if missing_keys:
        raise ValueError(
            f"Evaluation config is missing keys: {sorted(missing_keys)}"
        )

    list_fields = [
        "portfolio_metrics",
        "distributional_metrics",
        "uncertainty_metrics",
        "decision_support_metrics",
        "comparison_groups",
        "primary_metrics",
    ]

    for field_name in list_fields:
        if not isinstance(data[field_name], list):
            raise ValueError(f"evaluation.{field_name} must be a list")

        if len(data[field_name]) == 0:
            raise ValueError(f"evaluation.{field_name} must not be empty")

    required_primary_metrics = {"total_return", "sharpe", "max_drawdown", "cvar10"}
    primary_metrics = set(data["primary_metrics"])

    missing_primary_metrics = required_primary_metrics - primary_metrics

    if missing_primary_metrics:
        raise ValueError(
            "evaluation.primary_metrics must include: "
            f"{sorted(missing_primary_metrics)}"
        )


def load_evaluation_config_from_json(path: Path) -> EvaluationConfig:
    if not path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Evaluation config file does not exist: {path}")

    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
        data = json.load(file)

    return EvaluationConfig.from_dict(data)


def get_evaluation_config(
    evaluation_id: str | None = None,
) -> EvaluationConfig:
    selected_evaluation_id = evaluation_id or DEFAULT_EVALUATION_ID
    evaluation_path = EVALUATION_CONFIG_DIRECTORY / f"{selected_evaluation_id}.json"

    return load_evaluation_config_from_json(evaluation_path)


def list_available_evaluation_ids() -> tuple[str, ...]:
    if not EVALUATION_CONFIG_DIRECTORY.exists():
        return tuple()

    return tuple(
        sorted(path.stem for path in EVALUATION_CONFIG_DIRECTORY.glob("*.json"))
    )
```

## 3. Opdater `runner/run_smoke_test.py`

Erstat hele filen med denne:

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/runner/run_smoke_test.py

from __future__ import annotations

import json

from stock_investment_dss.evaluation.evaluation_config import get_evaluation_config
from stock_investment_dss.strategies.predefined import get_strategy
from stock_investment_dss.utilities.config import (
    get_boolean_environment_variable,
    get_environment_variable,
)
from stock_investment_dss.utilities.logging import (
    setup_run_logger,
    setup_system_logger,
)
from stock_investment_dss.utilities.paths import PROJECT_ROOT, create_run_paths
from stock_investment_dss.utilities.seed import set_global_seed


def write_json(path, data: dict) -> None:
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    with path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as file:
        json.dump(data, file, indent=2)


def main() -> int:
    log_level = get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_LOG_LEVEL",
        default="INFO",
    ) or "INFO"

    system_logger = setup_system_logger(log_level=log_level)
    system_logger.info("Starting StockInvestmentDSS smoke test.")
    system_logger.info("Project root: %s", PROJECT_ROOT)

    run_paths = None

    try:
        set_global_seed(42)

        default_strategy_id = get_environment_variable(
            "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_STRATEGY",
            default="balanced",
        )

        default_evaluation_id = get_environment_variable(
            "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_EVALUATION",
            default="default",
        )

        use_wandb = get_boolean_environment_variable(
            "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_USE_WANDB",
            default=False,
        )

        run_paths = create_run_paths("d_iqn_dss_smoke_test")
        run_logger = setup_run_logger(run_paths, log_level=log_level)

        run_logger.info("Created run directory: %s", run_paths.run_directory)
        run_logger.info("Run id: %s", run_paths.run_id)
        run_logger.info("Weights & Biases enabled: %s", use_wandb)

        strategy = get_strategy(default_strategy_id)
        evaluation_config = get_evaluation_config(default_evaluation_id)

        strategy_snapshot_path = run_paths.config_directory / "strategy.json"
        evaluation_snapshot_path = run_paths.config_directory / "evaluation.json"

        write_json(strategy_snapshot_path, strategy.to_dict())
        write_json(evaluation_snapshot_path, evaluation_config.to_dict())

        run_logger.info(
            "Loaded strategy: %s (%s)",
            strategy.strategy_id,
            strategy.display_name,
        )
        run_logger.info("Wrote strategy snapshot: %s", strategy_snapshot_path)

        run_logger.info(
            "Loaded evaluation config: %s",
            evaluation_config.evaluation_id,
        )
        run_logger.info("Wrote evaluation snapshot: %s", evaluation_snapshot_path)

        smoke_summary = {
            "status": "ok",
            "project_name": "StockInvestmentDSS",
            "prototype_name": "D-IQN-DSS",
            "prototype_full_name": (
                "Discrete Implicit Quantile Network for "
                "Stock Investment Decision Support"
            ),
            "run_id": run_paths.run_id,
            "project_root": str(PROJECT_ROOT),
            "run_directory": str(run_paths.run_directory),
            "wandb_enabled": use_wandb,
            "strategy": {
                "strategy_id": strategy.strategy_id,
                "display_name": strategy.display_name,
                "risk_profile": strategy.risk_profile,
                "objective": strategy.objective,
                "allowed_actions": list(strategy.allowed_actions),
            },
            "evaluation": {
                "evaluation_id": evaluation_config.evaluation_id,
                "primary_metrics": list(evaluation_config.primary_metrics),
                "portfolio_metrics": list(evaluation_config.portfolio_metrics),
                "distributional_metrics": list(
                    evaluation_config.distributional_metrics
                ),
                "uncertainty_metrics": list(evaluation_config.uncertainty_metrics),
                "decision_support_metrics": list(
                    evaluation_config.decision_support_metrics
                ),
            },
            "next_step": "Build FinRL data pipeline.",
        }

        summary_path = run_paths.summary_directory / "smoke_test_summary.json"
        write_json(summary_path, smoke_summary)

        run_logger.info("Wrote smoke test summary: %s", summary_path)
        system_logger.info("StockInvestmentDSS smoke test completed successfully.")

        return 0

    except Exception:
        system_logger.exception("StockInvestmentDSS smoke test failed.")

        if run_paths is not None:
            try:
                run_logger = setup_run_logger(run_paths, log_level=log_level)
                run_logger.exception("Run failed.")
            except Exception:
                pass

        return 1


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())
```

STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_EVALUATION=default

STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DATA_SOURCE=finrl

## 5. Kør smoke test

Fra projektroden:

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH="src"
python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.run_smoke_test
```

Forventet output i ny run-folder:

```text
outputs/runs/<run_id>/
├── config/
│   ├── strategy.json
│   └── evaluation.json
├── logs/
│   ├── errors.log
│   └── run.log
└── summary/
    └── smoke_test_summary.json
```

ChatGPT:

Ja — præcis.

Du skal erstatte den nuværende `run_smoke_test.py` med den version, du lige har pasted. Den nye version gør det, vi vil have nu:

```text
1. Opretter run folder
2. Loader default strategy fra .env
3. Loader default evaluation config fra .env
4. Gemmer snapshots:
   outputs/runs/<run_id>/config/strategy.json
   outputs/runs/<run_id>/config/evaluation.json
5. Skriver summary med strategy/evaluation metadata
```

Den pasted version importerer også de nye moduler:

```python
from stock_investment_dss.evaluation.evaluation_config import get_evaluation_config
from stock_investment_dss.strategies.predefined import get_strategy
```

så før du kører den, skal disse filer være på plads:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/schema.py
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined.py
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined/defensive.json
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined/balanced.json
src/stock_investment_dss/strategies/predefined/aggressive.json

src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/__init__.py
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/evaluation_config.py
src/stock_investment_dss/evaluation/configs/default.json
```

Og `.env` bør have:

```env
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_STRATEGY=balanced
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_DEFAULT_EVALUATION=default
```

Kør derefter:

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH="src"
python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.run_smoke_test
```

Forventet ny run-folder:

```text
outputs/runs/<timestamp>_d_iqn_dss_smoke_test/
├── config/
│   ├── strategy.json
│   └── evaluation.json
├── logs/
│   ├── errors.log
│   └── run.log
└── summary/
    └── smoke_test_summary.json
```

Hvis det fejler, er det sandsynligvis en af disse tre ting: `evaluation/__init__.py` mangler, `default.json` ligger et andet sted end `evaluation/configs/default.json`, eller strategy JSON-filerne ligger ikke i `strategies/predefined/`.

ChatGPT:

Jeg har nu gennemgået de relevante dele af de uploads, du pegede på:

```text
system.zip
src(2).zip
zero-sum-public-main (2).zip
FinRL-master.zip
data_Conversation.md
```

Min konklusion er ret klar:

> **Vi skal ikke bygge én gigantisk “hent alt data”-pipeline. Vi skal bygge en FinRL-first daily pipeline + et Zero-Sum-inspireret cache/on-demand intraday layer.**

Det passer bedst til din problemformulering, fordi FinRL skal være fundamentet for historisk market data og RL-environment, mens systemet samtidig skal kunne simulere near real-time, point-in-time decision support uden look-ahead bias. 

---

## Hvad jeg ser i de forskellige kodebaser

### `system.zip`

Det du tidligere byggede her er faktisk ret værdifuldt som **backend/data-service inspiration**.

Især disse idéer kan genbruges konceptuelt:

```text
- yfinance fallback hvis primær datakilde fejler
- normalisering af OHLCV-data
- DuckDB persistence
- FinRL-compatible export
- ingestion logs
```

Men jeg ville ikke flytte det direkte ind i den nye V2-kode nu. Det er for app/backend-orienteret til det trin, vi er i lige nu.

Det vigtigste vi tager med er:

```text
raw source data
↓
canonical internal schema
↓
FinRL-compatible dataframe
↓
logged ingestion
```

---

### `src(2).zip`

Den gamle research/V1-kode har mange brugbare idéer, men også den output/path-rod, vi netop har forsøgt at undgå.

Det vi tager med:

```text
- PIT-tankegang
- result summaries
- baselines
- action/decision visualizations
```

Det vi ikke tager med direkte:

```text
- single-AAPL assumption
- spredte output folders
- train_data/trade_data placeret mange steder
- runners der selv opfinder output paths
```

---

### `zero-sum-public-main (2).zip`

Det her repo er faktisk meget relevant.

Det laver ikke “magisk live trading data”. Det bruger primært:

```text
- yfinance historical candles
- yfinance fast_info / quote-lignende polling
- cache
- batch prefetch
- fallback fetch
- period/interval clamping
```

Det vigtigste designprincip derfra er:

> **Cache først. Fetch kun hvis cache mangler eller er stale.**

Det matcher præcis din PoC-idé: bruger vælger aktie/point-in-time, systemet viser daily/1h/15m/5m/1m efter hvad der findes, og henter kun on-demand når nødvendigt.

Det matcher også din tidligere data-samtale, hvor vi netop konkluderede, at daily skal være RL/backtest-master, mens intraday skal være UI-/forklaringslag og 1m helst bør være on-demand.

---

### `FinRL-master.zip`

FinRL-koden bekræfter, at vi skal bruge FinRL centralt til **daily master pipeline** og ikke prøve at tvinge hele intraday-laget gennem FinRL.

FinRL har:

```text
DataProcessor
YahooFinanceProcessor
YahooDownloader / yfinance integration
StockTradingEnv
Feature engineering
```

Men FinRL’s YahooFinanceProcessor er ikke ideel som generel intraday-cache-builder for 1h/15m/5m/1m. Den er bedre som **RL data foundation**, altså:

```text
daily OHLCV
technical indicators
VIX / turbulence where relevant
FinRL dataframe format
StockTradingEnv-compatible input
```

Så vores split bliver:

```text
FinRL = daily RL/backtest master
yfinance cache layer = intraday UI/context/on-demand
```

Det er også praktisk nødvendigt, fordi yfinance-dokumentationen angiver, at gyldige intervaller inkluderer fx `1m`, `5m`, `15m`, `60m`, `1h`, `1d`, men at intraday-data ikke kan række længere end de seneste 60 dage. ([ranaroussi.github.io][1])

---

## 1. `market_data_paths.py`

Formål:

```text
Ingen hardcoded data paths i data pipeline.
```

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/data/market_data_paths.py

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path

from stock_investment_dss.utilities.paths import DATA_DIRECTORY


MARKET_DATA_DIRECTORY = DATA_DIRECTORY / "market"

DAILY_DIRECTORY = MARKET_DATA_DIRECTORY / "daily"
DAILY_COMBINED_DIRECTORY = DAILY_DIRECTORY / "combined"
DAILY_PROCESSED_DIRECTORY = DAILY_DIRECTORY / "processed"

INTRADAY_DIRECTORY = MARKET_DATA_DIRECTORY / "intraday"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class DailyMarketDataPaths:
    dataset_id: str
    combined_file: Path
    train_file: Path
    validation_file: Path
    simulation_file: Path
    metadata_file: Path


def ensure_market_data_directories() -> None:
    for directory in [
        MARKET_DATA_DIRECTORY,
        DAILY_DIRECTORY,
        DAILY_COMBINED_DIRECTORY,
        DAILY_PROCESSED_DIRECTORY,
        INTRADAY_DIRECTORY,
    ]:
        directory.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)


def get_daily_market_data_paths(dataset_id: str) -> DailyMarketDataPaths:
    ensure_market_data_directories()

    safe_dataset_id = dataset_id.strip().lower()

    return DailyMarketDataPaths(
        dataset_id=safe_dataset_id,
        combined_file=DAILY_COMBINED_DIRECTORY
        / f"market_data_{safe_dataset_id}_1d.csv",
        train_file=DAILY_PROCESSED_DIRECTORY / f"train_data_{safe_dataset_id}_1d.csv",
        validation_file=DAILY_PROCESSED_DIRECTORY
        / f"validation_data_{safe_dataset_id}_1d.csv",
        simulation_file=DAILY_PROCESSED_DIRECTORY
        / f"simulation_data_{safe_dataset_id}_1d.csv",
        metadata_file=DAILY_COMBINED_DIRECTORY
        / f"market_data_{safe_dataset_id}_1d_metadata.json",
    )
```

---

## 2. `ticker_universes.py`

Først hardcoder vi demo-universet. Senere flytter vi det evt. til JSON.

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/data/ticker_universes.py

from __future__ import annotations


DEMO_5_TICKERS = ("AAPL", "MSFT", "NVDA", "SPY", "QQQ")


PREDEFINED_UNIVERSES: dict[str, tuple[str, ...]] = {
    "demo_5": DEMO_5_TICKERS,
}


def get_ticker_universe(universe_id: str) -> tuple[str, ...]:
    normalized_universe_id = universe_id.strip().lower()

    try:
        return PREDEFINED_UNIVERSES[normalized_universe_id]
    except KeyError as exc:
        available = ", ".join(sorted(PREDEFINED_UNIVERSES.keys()))
        raise ValueError(
            f"Unknown universe_id='{universe_id}'. Available: {available}"
        ) from exc
```

---

## 3. `finrl_data_pipeline.py`

Denne første version bruger yfinance direkte, men outputter **FinRL-compatible format**. Næste version kan skifte til FinRL `YahooDownloader`/`DataProcessor`, men dette er den mest robuste start, fordi vi straks får kontrol over cache, source, errors og metadata.

```python
# src/stock_investment_dss/data/finrl_data_pipeline.py

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Iterable

import pandas as pd
import yfinance as yf

from stock_investment_dss.data.market_data_paths import (
    DailyMarketDataPaths,
    get_daily_market_data_paths,
)
from stock_investment_dss.data.ticker_universes import get_ticker_universe


FINRL_DAILY_COLUMNS = [
    "date",
    "tic",
    "open",
    "high",
    "low",
    "close",
    "adj_close",
    "volume",
    "day",
    "source",
    "downloaded_at",
]


def _normalize_yfinance_daily_frame(
    raw_frame: pd.DataFrame,
    ticker: str,
    source: str,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    if raw_frame is None or raw_frame.empty:
        return pd.DataFrame(columns=FINRL_DAILY_COLUMNS)

    frame = raw_frame.copy()
    frame = frame.reset_index()

    frame.columns = [
        str(column).strip().lower().replace(" ", "_")
        for column in frame.columns
    ]

    date_column = None
    for candidate in ["date", "datetime", "index"]:
        if candidate in frame.columns:
            date_column = candidate
            break

    if date_column is None:
        raise ValueError(
            f"Could not find date column for {ticker}. "
            f"Columns: {list(frame.columns)}"
        )

    rename_candidates = {
        "open": "open",
        "high": "high",
        "low": "low",
        "close": "close",
        "adj_close": "adj_close",
        "adjclose": "adj_close",
        "volume": "volume",
    }

    for source_column, target_column in rename_candidates.items():
        if source_column in frame.columns and target_column not in frame.columns:
            frame[target_column] = frame[source_column]

    if "adj_close" not in frame.columns:
        frame["adj_close"] = frame["close"]

    required = ["open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"]
    missing = [column for column in required if column not in frame.columns]

    if missing:
        raise ValueError(
            f"Missing required OHLCV columns for {ticker}: {missing}. "
            f"Columns: {list(frame.columns)}"
        )

    output = pd.DataFrame(
        {
            "date": pd.to_datetime(frame[date_column], errors="coerce"),
            "tic": ticker.upper(),
            "open": pd.to_numeric(frame["open"], errors="coerce"),
            "high": pd.to_numeric(frame["high"], errors="coerce"),
            "low": pd.to_numeric(frame["low"], errors="coerce"),
            "close": pd.to_numeric(frame["close"], errors="coerce"),
            "adj_close": pd.to_numeric(frame["adj_close"], errors="coerce"),
            "volume": pd.to_numeric(frame["volume"], errors="coerce"),
            "source": source,
            "downloaded_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        }
    )

    output = output.dropna(subset=["date", "open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"])
    output["date"] = output["date"].dt.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
    output["day"] = pd.to_datetime(output["date"]).dt.dayofweek
    output["volume"] = output["volume"].astype("int64")

    return output[FINRL_DAILY_COLUMNS]


def download_daily_market_data(
    tickers: Iterable[str],
    start_date: str,
    end_date: str,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    frames: list[pd.DataFrame] = []

    for ticker in tickers:
        ticker_upper = ticker.strip().upper()

        if not ticker_upper:
            continue

        raw = yf.download(
            ticker_upper,
            start=start_date,
            end=end_date,
            interval="1d",
            auto_adjust=False,
            progress=False,
            threads=False,
        )

        normalized = _normalize_yfinance_daily_frame(
            raw_frame=raw,
            ticker=ticker_upper,
            source="yfinance:daily",
        )

        if not normalized.empty:
            frames.append(normalized)

    if not frames:
        return pd.DataFrame(columns=FINRL_DAILY_COLUMNS)

    data = pd.concat(frames, ignore_index=True)
    data = data.sort_values(["date", "tic"]).reset_index(drop=True)

    return data


def load_or_download_daily_market_data(
    universe_id: str,
    start_date: str,
    end_date: str,
    force_download: bool = False,
) -> tuple[pd.DataFrame, DailyMarketDataPaths]:
    paths = get_daily_market_data_paths(universe_id)

    if paths.combined_file.exists() and not force_download:
        data = pd.read_csv(paths.combined_file)
        return data, paths

    tickers = get_ticker_universe(universe_id)
    data = download_daily_market_data(
        tickers=tickers,
        start_date=start_date,
        end_date=end_date,
    )

    paths.combined_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    data.to_csv(paths.combined_file, index=False)

    metadata = {
        "dataset_id": universe_id,
        "frequency": "1d",
        "start_date": start_date,
        "end_date": end_date,
        "tickers": list(tickers),
        "row_count": int(len(data)),
        "columns": list(data.columns),
        "created_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        "source": "yfinance",
        "format": "finrl_compatible_daily",
    }

    with paths.metadata_file.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as file:
        json.dump(metadata, file, indent=2)

    return data, paths
```

---

# Små, men vigtige valg her

Jeg starter ikke med intraday i samme fil.

Det kommer i:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/data/intraday_cache.py
```

efter daily virker.

Det er bevidst. Din egen data-samtale sagde også, at daily FinRL-pipeline og intraday yfinance cache bør være adskilte scripts/layers.

# Opdateret smoke test efter dette

Når de tre filer er lavet, kan vi udvide `run_smoke_test.py` med:

```python
from stock_investment_dss.data.finrl_data_pipeline import (
    load_or_download_daily_market_data,
)
```

og efter strategy/evaluation snapshot:

```python
daily_data, daily_paths = load_or_download_daily_market_data(
    universe_id="demo_5",
    start_date="2024-01-01",
    end_date="2024-03-01",
    force_download=False,
)

data_snapshot_path = run_paths.data_directory / "market_data_demo_5_1d.csv"
daily_data.to_csv(data_snapshot_path, index=False)

run_logger.info(
    "Loaded daily market data: rows=%s columns=%s",
    len(daily_data),
    list(daily_data.columns),
)
run_logger.info("Wrote run data snapshot: %s", data_snapshot_path)
```

Og i summary:

```python
"data": {
    "universe_id": "demo_5",
    "frequency": "1d",
    "row_count": int(len(daily_data)),
    "columns": list(daily_data.columns),
    "cache_file": str(daily_paths.combined_file),
}
```

---

# Men før du indsætter smoke-test ændringen

Først opret de tre datafiler:

```text
market_data_paths.py
ticker_universes.py
finrl_data_pipeline.py
```

Så kører vi en separat hurtig test:

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH="src"
python -c "from stock_investment_dss.data.finrl_data_pipeline import load_or_download_daily_market_data; df,p=load_or_download_daily_market_data('demo_5','2024-01-01','2024-03-01'); print(df.head()); print(df.shape); print(p.combined_file)"
```

Hvis den virker, kobler vi den ind i smoke testen.

---

# Retningen herfra

Vi bygger data-laget i tre trin:

```text
Step DATA-1:
Daily demo_5 FinRL-compatible cache

Step DATA-2:
Daily PIT splits: train / validation / simulation

Step DATA-3:
Intraday cache:
1h, 15m, 5m, 1m-on-demand
```

Så nu er næste konkrete action:

```text
DATA-1: implementér daily FinRL-compatible market data cache.
```

Det er den rigtige første sten i FinRL Data Pipeline.

[1]: https://ranaroussi.github.io/yfinance/reference/api/yfinance.download.html?utm_source=chatgpt.com "yfinance.download"

"
3. finrl_data_pipeline.py

Denne første version bruger yfinance direkte, men outputter FinRL-compatible format. Næste version kan skifte til FinRL YahooDownloader/DataProcessor, men dette er den mest robuste start, fordi vi straks får kontrol over cache, source, errors og metadata.
"

ChatGPT:


Ja — du har ret.

Hvis din professor siger:

```text
DATA = FinRL
```

så skal vi **ikke** starte med “vores egen yfinance-pipeline” og først bagefter skifte til FinRL.

Det var forkert prioriteret af mig.

Den rigtige V2-retning er:

```text
FinRL først
egen cache/logik rundt om FinRL
ikke egen data-pipeline i stedet for FinRL
```

Din projektbeskrivelse siger også direkte, at **FinRL er det primære data framework**, og at det fungerer som foundation for historical market data og RL-environment setup. 

Så ja: vi skal bygge `finrl_data_pipeline.py` som en **FinRL wrapper**, ikke som en separat yfinance-downloader.

---

## Korrekt princip

Ikke:

```text
yfinance direkte
↓
FinRL-compatible format
↓
måske FinRL senere
```

Men:

```text
FinRL data processor / YahooDownloader / FeatureEngineer
↓
vores cache + metadata + logs
↓
vores PIT splits
↓
vores environment / DSS pipeline
```

Det er meget mere forsvarligt akademisk.

---

# Ny beslutning for data-laget

Vi bygger:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/data/finrl_data_pipeline.py
```

som:

```text
FinRL-first data pipeline
```

Den skal gøre:

```text
1. Bruge FinRL til daily market data
2. Bruge FinRL FeatureEngineer til tekniske indikatorer
3. Gemme output i vores data/market/... struktur
4. Gemme metadata
5. Logge fejl i system/data pipeline logs
6. Returnere dataframe til resten af StockInvestmentDSS
```

Så kan vi stadig have vores egen cache og filstruktur, men **datahentning og feature engineering skal så vidt muligt ske gennem FinRL**.

---

# Hvad med Zero Sum-inspirationen?

Zero Sum er stadig relevant, men kun til **intraday/cache/live-ish UI-laget**.

Så skellet bliver:

```text
Core thesis / RL / backtest data:
FinRL

PoC UI / intraday context / quote polling:
Zero-Sum-inspireret cache/on-demand layer
```

Altså:

```text
FinRL daily pipeline
↓
RL training, validation, simulation, backtesting

Intraday cache layer
↓
UI charts, point-in-time explanation, recent context
```

Det er stærkere end at lade yfinance overtage hele data-laget.

---

# Rigtig arkitektur nu

```text
FinRL Data Pipeline
    ↓
FinRL FeatureEngineer
    ↓
Cached FinRL daily master dataset
    ↓
Point-in-time split
    ↓
FinRL-style portfolio environment
    ↓
Current portfolio state
    ↓
Investor strategy config
    ↓
Action generator / action mask
    ↓
IQN estimates return distributions
    ↓
Evidential uncertainty estimates model confidence
    ↓
Risk policy scores actions
    ↓
Recommendation engine
    ↓
Audit log
    ↓
Common evaluation suite
```

Og parallelt senere:

```text
Intraday cache / quote layer
    ↓
PoC UI explanation
    ↓
Point-in-time charts
```

---

# Hvad skal vi ændre i næste kodeforslag?

Jeg ville droppe den tidligere direkte `yf.download(...)` version.

I stedet skal første `finrl_data_pipeline.py` være bygget omkring noget i denne stil:

```python
from finrl.meta.preprocessor.yahoodownloader import YahooDownloader
from finrl.meta.preprocessor.preprocessors import FeatureEngineer
```

eller via FinRL’s `DataProcessor`, afhængigt af hvad der virker mest stabilt i din installerede FinRL-version.

Målet for første version:

```text
Universe: demo_5
Tickers: AAPL, MSFT, NVDA, SPY, QQQ
Start: 2024-01-01
End: 2024-03-01
Source: FinRL YahooDownloader
Features: FinRL FeatureEngineer
Output: data/market/daily/combined/market_data_demo_5_1d.csv
Snapshot: outputs/runs/<run_id>/data/market_data_demo_5_1d.csv
```

---

# Hvad med yfinance direkte?

Det må stadig eksistere, men ikke som hovedspor.

Jeg ville placere direkte yfinance i en senere fil:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/data/intraday_cache.py
```

eller:

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/data/quote_cache.py
```

Men den skal ikke være `finrl_data_pipeline.py`.

Det bliver:

```text
finrl_data_pipeline.py = FinRL daily master data
intraday_cache.py      = Zero-Sum-inspireret UI/context data
```

---

# Kort sagt

Ja, din indvending er korrekt.

Vi skal ikke bygge “vores egen data-pipeline” først.

Vi skal bygge:

```text
FinRL-first data pipeline
```

med vores egen:

```text
cache
metadata
logging
path discipline
PIT split
snapshotting
```

uden at erstatte FinRL.

Så næste skridt bør være, at jeg giver dig en ny `finrl_data_pipeline.py`, der bruger FinRL direkte som datakilde og feature engineering — ikke `yf.download` direkte.
